Letter Received:

Having read in your esteemed newspaper on October 4th the special Tianjin dispatch on the 3rd which said, "The Tianjin-Pukou Railway dispatching telephone line between Tianjin and Yangliuqing was cut off for six kilometers for unknown reasons," the facts are considerably inconsistent. It has been discovered the affairs telephone between Liangwangzhuang to Yangliuqing line did indeed on the evening of September 27th at 8 o'clock some, be found broken at Shuangzhan six sections, for approximately three hundred meters. This was immediately addressed by dispatching workers to rush to repair it, and by 12:10AM that night, communications were restored. Vehicle transit was not impacted. Thus, on October 3rd, there was no case of telephone wire being cut off. Fearing that rumours would cause miscommunication, we specially send this letter, please investigate and correct it. Respectfully, Tianjin-Pukou Railway Vehicle Affairs Office. October 5th.

Review of Trade Surplus, Trade Deficit, and Our Country's Trade Surplus and Deficit (Part 2)

— Luo Dunwei

——Speech on the Central Broadcasting Station——

First, let's examine the main countries involved in our country's trade: Although Portugal and Spain were the earliest in modern international trade with our country, Britain was the first to formally establish agencies to protect trade. In 1684, Britain obtained permission from the Qing court to establish a trading post in Guangzhou, officially opening trade. After the Opium War, the Treaty of Nanjing was signed, obtaining the cession of Hong Kong and the convenience of five trading ports. British trade with our country flourished even more. Later, with the establishment of various unequal treaties for Tianjin, Yantai, Burma, and Tibet, Britain's commercial power could be said to have dominated East Asia. After the Sino-Japanese War, Japan gained independence for Korea (it was independent at that time), and acquired Taiwan and the Penghu Islands, leading to a rapid increase in trade with our country. Later, after the Russo-Japanese War and the annexation of Korea, Japan could compete with Britain. During the European War, taking advantage of the fact that various countries had no energy to attend to East Asia, Japan dominated for a time, taking first place in trade with China. After the end of the European War, the United States, due to the war, transformed from a debtor nation to a creditor nation. The so-called "permanent prosperity" in the economic sphere reached everywhere in the world, and it also seized the first place in trade with our country. Japan had to retreat to second place. (See attached table)

Second, let's now discuss import and export commodities: Our country's important import commodities were originally mainly opium, woollen cloth, and hardware. Later, the import of British cotton fabrics increased. In 1870, the import of cotton goods accounted for one percent of our total imports. Until before the European War, cotton goods were always the most imported item by Britain into our country. As a result, the basic work of "female weaving" in our country's agriculture was defeated, naturally posing a major threat to the countryside. Since the beginning of the Republic of China, international imperialism has been able to infiltrate our economy in every way, so the imported goods have become particularly complex, with almost everything available. In recent years, even coffins for the dead have been imported. The foreign-style steel coffins that you have seen in funeral homes are made of imported materials. What is particularly noteworthy is the increased import of food and the decrease in the export of agricultural products in recent years. In the 22nd year of the Republic of China, the total value of imported rice and wheat was close to 200 million yuan. The amount of food imported annually is still very large now. Needless to say, the import of cotton is also very large. It ranked first in the 21st year of the Republic of China, reaching 180,782,997 yuan. Thus, "male farming," a basic condition in our country's economy, has also been threatened. Exports are even more dangerous. Our country's exports have always been dominated by silk and tea; soybeans also accounted for a considerable amount. Initially, silk and tea accounted for 80% of the total value of exports. Later, due to competition from Japanese and French silk and tea, it fell to 50% in 1898, and has become even worse in recent years. Soybeans have accounted for a large proportion of export commodities in recent years, sometimes ranking first. The situation completely changed after the "September 18th" Incident; in the 22nd year, it turned into a trade deficit. Recently, due to the increase in tung oil exports, the situation is a little better, but as of now, there has been no major turnaround in the export of silk and tea. Moreover, recently, I studied the import of luxury goods and found that the annual import of items such as tobacco and alcohol is very large. The average is always around 40 million yuan per year, with tobacco imports being the largest. It accounted for more than 19 million yuan in the 22nd year and more than 14 million yuan in the 23rd year. These statements all show the severity of our country's economic ailments, so everyone should pay special attention.

Third, let's analyze the methods to offset our country's trade deficit: Our country's trade deficit is very large: even in the last five years alone, it has exceeded 3.1 billion yuan of silver. Can it offset this five-year trade deficit? However, in fact, since the establishment of the Republic of China, silver imports have always been greater than exports, which is a trade deficit. In the last five years, the 21st and 22nd years of the Republic of China were still trade deficits; the 22nd, 23rd, and 24th years were trade surpluses. However, the amount is still limited. Even adding the smuggling of silver, it is not very large. In any case, it is far from the aforementioned 3.1 billion yuan. Therefore, according to general research, the methods to offset our country's trade deficit are roughly as follows: Cultural expenses of foreigners in China; Expenses of foreigners traveling to China; Expenses of foreign troops stationed in China; Foreign investment in China; Remittances from overseas Chinese. Among the five offsetting methods above, the first, second, and third are very small. Moreover, the third is greatly detrimental to our country. The fourth, the way foreign capital has been used in the past is incorrect and has only helped to fuel imperialist aggression. The only legitimate and beneficial offsetting method for our country is the fifth, remittances from overseas Chinese. It is true that remittances from overseas Chinese are a major offsetting method in our country's international balance, which is known to everyone. However, there is no consistent estimate of the exact amount. Dr. Morse estimated it at 110 million yuan in 1903. Remer, based on his own investigation, estimated an average of about 300 million yuan per year in 1928, 1929, and 1930. In the past five years, the Bank of China has estimated overseas Chinese remittances; the lowest is 200 million yuan, and the highest can reach 390 million yuan. The highest was in 1931, and the lowest was in 1933. In the past two years, it has been around 290 million yuan. Recently, Mr. Xing Chengxi published an estimate in the Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Institute's special publication, estimating that overseas Chinese remittances in the past five years were over 400 million yuan in 1931; 320 million yuan in 1932; 305 million yuan in 1933; fell to 250 million yuan in 1934; and rose again to 316 million yuan in 1935. Although the estimates of various sources differ in size, the average annual remittance from overseas Chinese is generally around 300 million yuan, which seems to be reasonably accurate. Adding the various offsetting methods above, it should be around 500 million yuan per year. From this, it seems that the 500 million yuan trade deficit can be offset. It should be known that in addition to this, we pay about 100 million yuan in foreign debt each year; the purchase of military supplies and the sending of students to study abroad cost about 50 to 100 million yuan each year. Therefore, offsetting China's international balance of payments is still a problem. The most urgent thing to note is that among the above offsetting methods, only remittances from overseas Chinese are a healthy method. However, this healthy method has been gradually declining due to the everywhere people discrimination against overseas Chinese and other political and economic reasons, which makes us feel the severity of this offsetting problem even more.

From the above explanations, we can know that although a trade deficit is not necessarily harmful to the country in theory, our country's international trade deficit is, first, because the amount is too large and cannot be offset; second, because the imported goods are all daily necessities, consumer goods, and luxury goods, while production tools are very few; from whichever aspect we look at it, it cannot be said to be a sign of promoting collapse for the entire national economy. Therefore, although we cannot uniformly prohibit the use of foreign goods, we hope that everyone will pay attention to Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industry's statement: "Production tools are welcome as foreign goods, consumer goods must use domestic goods." (The End)

Page 5

Current Affairs Commentary

Opening of the Annual Meeting of the China Cooperation Society

— Willow

The Chinese cooperative movement began seventeen years ago. Mr. Xue Xianzhou founded the National Cooperative Savings Bank Civilian School, which served as its banner. Since the Nationalist Party came to power, it has been eager to promote cooperative enterprises to achieve the socialization of distribution. Cooperation has been listed as one of the seven major movements. The China Cooperation Society was also established with the advocacy of Mr. Chen Guofu, Mr. Wang Shiying and others. The society takes the investigation, research, promotion, and guidance of cooperative undertakings as its mission. It has been nearly eight years since its establishment. The number of members has increased from twenty-two to four hundred and thirty-six. The society has published the Cooperative Monthly, disseminated cooperative knowledge, guided cooperative operations, established the Xianzhou Library to store cooperative books, jointly organized training classes for cooperative personnel, and promoted cooperative undertakings. These few points have already demonstrated the intensity of its work. The fifth annual meeting of the Cooperative Society was held in Changsha. The members, based on their usual research, should be able to take this opportunity to make many new contributions.

However, the implementation of a business or system must have its foundation. We should guide it by adapting to the circumstances. If the situation is favorable, we should supervise and encourage each other to teach and transform. If the situation is difficult, cooperation in China seems to lack this foundation. However, mutual aid associations are indeed a form of credit cooperation. Community granaries are a form of disaster prevention cooperation. Community schools are a form of educational cooperation. Mutual vigilance and assistance are a form of security cooperation. The land associations (gatherings of neighborhood communities) held in rural areas are a form of local business cooperation. However, their organizations are crude. Although there are rules to follow, they do not suit the complex era of modern personnel affairs. Therefore, when discussing cooperative enterprises today, we should correct the defects and highlight the characteristics of existing systems and enterprises that embody the spirit of cooperation. In new areas, we should conduct in-depth publicity and seek broad public sympathy. We should advance on both fronts, embracing both the new and the old. Although planning may require more effort, it will be easier to achieve results during implementation.

Currently, the most pressing need is how to revitalize the countryside. Those who talk about revitalization often focus on the countryside itself, failing to realize that it is a complete economic issue that cannot be effectively addressed by partial treatment. However, this year, the prices of agricultural products such as soybeans, sesame, wheat, rapeseed, and cotton are all high. Farmers' incomes are higher than in previous years, and their lives are certainly more prosperous. At the same time, rice and grain have recovered greatly. This is truly an opportunity for rural areas to improve. What we are worried about is how to preserve their products and sell them at good prices. If we can plan for storage, transportation, and sales, provide cooperative organizations, and offer economic assistance, guiding them to have hope of success, farmers will naturally be happy to participate. In the past, the China Cooperation Society guided the cooperative enterprises in the Guangfu Temple area, and the results were remarkable. We hope to expand and broaden it, and extend it to various places.

Rural lending is rampant, but how much real benefit can farmers receive? Those who lend certainly have their difficulties. But if they do not break away from the exploitative model, how are they different from those who engage in high-interest loans? The most difficult thing for farmers today is economic injection and turnover. The old mutual aid association system has collapsed in nine out of ten cases due to rural bankruptcy. High-interest loans are harmful to farmers and have been suppressed. As the outcry against high-interest loans grows louder, the avenues for farmers to borrow money become narrower. Since the decline of pawnshops in the market, the value of pawned items has also been depreciated. Farmers cannot obtain what they need for production, nor can they obtain what they need for consumption. This situation has not yet been resolved. Therefore, if we do not plan and remedy the personnel aspects of farmers at the same time, then what is used for production will be in vain. For example, if rural borrowing aims to revitalize the countryside, but there is no intermediary organization, how can the process be fully beneficial? Therefore, supplementing deficiencies and correcting malpractices to benefit farmers is also the contribution of the China Cooperation Society in research and promotion.

We believe that the effectiveness of cooperative undertakings is not limited to this. It is undeniable that grassroots organizations are scattered. It is also difficult to avoid prioritizing personal interests over public interests. The promotion of cooperative undertakings can improve the organization, improve lives, and strengthen the economy. This is what the China Cooperation Society should strive for.

U.S. Secretary of the Navy Announces: Naval Policy Unchanged; Election Results Will Not Affect; Determined to Achieve Equality with the Strongest Country

Secretary of the Navy Swanson published an article in the Naval Magazine today, stating that U.S. naval policy will continue regardless of the outcome of the future presidential election. Although the White House occupants may change, the U.S. Navy must be equal to the strongest country. This right has been recognized by people at home and abroad. The recently concluded London Naval Treaty has many omissions. It is difficult to predict the future of naval construction. However, we will not hesitate to engage in naval competition. The conclusion states that if other countries disregard the 1930 London Naval Treaty and build excess warships, our naval strength will be hit and our security will be threatened. We will definitely rise up and compete with them. (National Telegram, 5th)

Honolulu. Rear Admiral Harnell, Commander of the U.S. Asiatic Fleet, took the mail steamer President Coolidge from here today to Manila to take up his new post. After the former Commander of the Asiatic Fleet, Muffin, arrives here, the handover will take place. The Current League of Nations Assembly Will Come to a Hasty End; The Disarmament Conference Presidium Meets; The Danzig Issue Asks Poland to Be Cautious; Accuses Britain of Poor Governance in Palestine

(Geneva) The Third Committee of the League of Nations Assembly, namely the Disarmament Committee, held a meeting in the afternoon to discuss the French proposal to convene the presidium of the Disarmament Conference. Representatives from Northern European countries immediately supported this proposal. French representative Boncour then spoke, saying that the most important task of the Disarmament Conference is to limit armaments. The first step is for the countries concerned to publicly announce their military budget figures as much as possible. At this point, British representative MacDonald, the Overseas Dominion Minister, declared that the British military reorganization is intended to ensure the safety of the country and fulfill its responsibilities to the British Empire, and is not used to promote aggressive policies. "If other countries do not agree to reduce military expenditures, Britain will not stop its military expansion plan." (Havas Telegram, 5th)

(Geneva) The French proposal to reconvene the presidium of the Disarmament Conference is now being discussed by the Third Committee of the League of Nations Assembly, namely the Disarmament Committee. It is reported that representatives from Britain and small countries in Northern Europe have expressed their support for the French proposal. The British and French delegations are currently drafting a resolution on this matter. In addition, the Third Committee will continue to meet on Wednesday this week to discuss. (Havas Telegram, 5th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Mandates Commission met today and its members criticized Britain's poor handling of Palestine. Norwegian representative Lange said that the entire Palestine is now a sacrifice to extremist Arab Nationalists and agitators. It is surprising that the trustee country cannot stop the violence. It is now appropriate to convene a special meeting of the Mandates Commission to discuss ways to clean up the situation. The Polish representative then spoke, hoping that Britain would maintain the policy of a Jewish national home, but said that he would propose a proposal to deal with the vast reserved areas for Jews in Northern and Eastern Europe, which is a major issue for Poland. (Reuters Telegram, 6th)

(Geneva) The Sixth Committee of the League of Nations Assembly, namely the Political Issues Committee, held a meeting this morning to discuss the issue of mandated territories. France was represented by Foreign Minister Weygand. First, Norwegian representative Lange expressed his congratulations on the recent treaty signed between France and Syria (a French mandated territory), which allowed Syria to establish an independent country three years later. However, he expressed concern about the conflict between the Jewish and Arab communities in Palestine. Next, Polish representative Komarnicki, on behalf of the Polish government, expressed the hope that Jewish settlements in Palestine should continue to exist, and that the British government should not prevent Jews from immigrating to Palestine in the future. Weygand then concluded the debate, stating that the British government hoped to find a compromise plan to take care of the legitimate interests of both the Arab and Jewish communities in order to resolve the current disputes. (Havas Telegram, 6th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council recently discussed the issue of the Free City of Danzig. Chairman Rivas of Chile and Lord Cranborne of Britain put forward a draft resolution, which stated, "The League of Nations High Commissioner in Danzig, Rösing (who has been transferred to the position of Deputy Secretary-General of the League of Nations), recently stated in his report that he had encountered various obstacles in performing his duties. The League of Nations Administrative Council hereby requests the Polish government to stop this, so that the guarantees provided by the League of Nations for the current system of the Free City will not become a mere formality. The Council believes that the Danzig issue is of utmost importance and is now preparing to hold a special meeting to discuss it." (Havas Telegram, 5th)

Danzig. International Labor Maritime Conference Opens; China Proposes to Include on Agenda Early; Equal Treatment of Seamen, Elimination of Contractor System

(Geneva) This morning, the International Labor Maritime Conference opened. Zhao Banfu, the Chinese labor representative, submitted a draft proposal, advocating that the case of equal treatment of foreign and domestic seamen should be included on the agenda as soon as possible, so as to formulate a convention to be followed uniformly. He also advocated that the contractor system implemented by foreign shipping companies in China should be abolished. The draft proposal generally stated that the 20th resolution of the International Labor Conference has decided to include the issue of the recruitment and treatment of foreign workers on the agenda as soon as possible, and the International Labor Report also advocates that foreign and domestic seamen should be treated equally to avoid capital from gaining undue benefits through international competition. Foreign shipping companies have been implementing this in China for a long time. Although the Chinese government has adopted strict methods, workers are afraid of losing their jobs and dare not resist even if they are oppressed. It is requested that this conference ask the governments of various countries to cooperate with the Chinese government to abolish this system. (Central News Agency Telegram, 6th)

Hungarian Prime Minister Dies; Cabinet Resigns; The Whole Country Mourns the News; Negotiations Underway for Candidates to Form a Cabinet

Budapest. Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös suffered from uremia and went to Munich, Germany for treatment on the 3rd of last month. He suddenly died at 9:40 this morning. Therefore, the cabinet may be reorganized immediately. There is talk that Agriculture Minister Darányi, who is currently acting as Prime Minister, will succeed Gömbös in organizing a new cabinet. (Havas Telegram, 6th)

Budapest. After the Hungarian government received the bad news of Gömbös' death, it submitted its resignation today. It is generally expected that there will be no serious political unrest, and there will be no major changes in Hungary's policies. (Reuters Telegram, 6th)

Budapest. After the bad news of Prime Minister Gömbös' death came, the cabinet immediately held a meeting, chaired by the acting Prime Minister and Minister of Agriculture Darányi. After the meeting, the acting Prime Minister also met with Regent Admiral Horthy and submitted the cabinet's resignation. Horthy is scheduled to meet with Cardinal Serédi, National Unity Party leader Iványi, Smallholders Party leader Eckhardt, and former Prime Minister Bethlen this afternoon to discuss candidates to form a cabinet. The entire city lowered flags to half-mast today, and all theaters and cinemas stopped performing. The radio station also stopped broadcasting to express mourning. (Havas Telegram, 6th)

(Rome) After the bad news of Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös' death came, people here mourned him because Gömbös was instrumental in the formation of the Rome Agreement between Italy, Austria, and Hungary. (Havas Telegram, 6th)

(Berlin) Hungarian Minister of Education Dr. Hóman is currently in Germany negotiating a cultural agreement between Germany and Austria. When Prime Minister Gömbös of Hungary was on his deathbed in the city of monks, he immediately reported the bad news of the Prime Minister's death to German leader Hitler, Aviation Minister Göring, and Hungarian Regent Admiral Horthy. Leader Hitler and General Göring immediately telegraphed Admiral Horthy and Mrs. Gömbös to express their condolences. Hóman told reporters that Germany and Hungary have a long-standing friendship. It is my duty to report the bad news of the Prime Minister to the German authorities. Our people mourn the loss of their leader. We hope that God will bless our people so that they can calmly deal with this change. (Havas Telegram, 6th)

Gömbös' Brief Biography

Munich. Hungarian Prime Minister and Minister of the Army General Gömbös died of illness today at a sanatorium near here, at the age of forty-nine. The general has been a powerful figure in Hungary for nearly seven years. His opponents regarded him as a National Socialist. Although the general tried his best to deny that he intended to implement a dictatorship, he admired Mussolini and Hitler's political skills and did not shy away from it. After going to Germany several times, he would often praise Hitler when talking to people. The general was the son of a village headmaster in a poor village. After graduating from military school, he worked in the Croatian Infantry Regiment. When the European War broke out in 1914, he served as a staff officer in the Chekelic White Army Corps and received the Third Class Medal for his contributions. In 1916, he was wounded during a night attack by the Russian army and returned to Budapest. After recovering, he worked in the Ministry of the Army. He was then ordered to go to Vienna. At that time, he wrote a booklet entitled "The Hungarian Army", advocating the establishment of an independent Hungarian army. During the Hungarian Revolution of 1918, he was ordered to return to the capital. Later, because he was proficient in foreign languages, he went to Cheklike to serve as a military commissioner. At the end of that year, he returned to the capital and was in charge of the so-called "Balkan Regiment" in the Ministry of the Army. Because he opposed the then President, Count Károlyi, he was listed as a retired officer when the Bolshevik Party came to power the following year. He then fled to Vienna and published a counter-revolutionary newspaper called the Hungarian Post. Soon after, he went to Chegeut, the stronghold of the counter-revolutionary "White Army", and served as the head of the White Army government. He was then forced to leave the area by France. While traveling to Vienna, he received news of the collapse of the Hungarian Red government and re-entered the Hungarian army, taking up a certain position. The following year, in 1920, he was elected as a member of parliament. In 1929, he served as Minister of the Army until his death. One year later, he was promoted to General. In 1932, he took the position of Prime Minister and made revising the peace treaty a part of the government's program. His policy was to form a new group of five countries: Germany, Italy, Poland, Austria, and Hungary. The general had recently suffered from heart disease and originally intended to resign today, but he died before he could submit his resignation. (Reuters Telegram, 6th)

Implementation of the Italian Currency Devaluation: Germany and Hungary Express Dissatisfaction; Italy Decides to Issue Special Public Bonds to Develop Abyssinian Resources; Pittman Supports Currency Agreement

(Rome) Yesterday's State Council decided on various measures to be taken when devaluing the currency. The first item stated that property owners, unaffected by the currency devaluation, should immediately subscribe to public bonds in an amount equal to 5% of the property's value. Regarding this, a responsible official has stated that the government has decided to issue special public bonds to be subscribed to by property owners. The funds will be used to develop Abyssinian resources, strengthen national defense expenditures, and levy a property tax to repay the principal and interest on these public bonds. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

(Rome) Following the devaluation of the Italian lira, the exchange market has temporarily suspended trading. It has now been decided to resume business tomorrow morning. Furthermore, after the implementation of the devaluation measures, the existing clearing agreements between Italy and other countries have automatically ceased to be effective. From now on, they should be implemented in accordance with the new lira exchange rate. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

(Rome) After the government decided to devalue the lira, it immediately notified the other two signatory countries of the Rome Agreement, namely Austria and Hungary, stating that the government would continue to maintain and promote mutual trade between Austria, Hungary, and Italy. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

(Paris) The financial circles here were not surprised by the news of the Italian lira devaluation. The financial circles here had already anticipated the devaluation of the lira when the Italian government announced that it would hold a State Council meeting today. Economic figures here believe that Italy's move "may contribute to peace," as it shows that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini intends to participate in international joint efforts to develop international trade through mutual coordination among countries. If this is the case, its impact on the overall situation will be significant. Furthermore, Italy's foreign trade was previously restricted due to special measures taken by the government. In the future, the lira devaluation will greatly increase export trade. (Havas News Agency, 5th)

(Berlin) People here are very surprised and uneasy after Italy devalued its currency and reduced import taxes. Responsible officials have stated that, except for coal, most of Germany's exports to Italy are manufactured goods. Although Italy has reduced import taxes on raw materials and food, it will not benefit German exports. Furthermore, Germany's economic policy is based on self-sufficiency and is maintained by the government's use of dictatorial power to implement a sound economic system. Now that Italy has devalued its currency, Germany is the only major industrial country that maintains the current value of its currency, and its economic policy has become isolated, causing a psychological blow. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

(Vienna) After the Italian government implemented the currency devaluation, it immediately notified Austria and Hungary, expressing its willingness to continue close cooperation with those countries. Political figures here have expressed great interest in this statement, saying that the meeting to be held here at the beginning of the month by the foreign ministers of Italy, Austria, and Hungary is becoming increasingly important. In addition, Finance Minister Traslau and National Bank President Kienbock discussed the new international monetary situation last night. According to political figures' predictions, although many in Austrian industry and commerce advocate for the devaluation of the Austrian schilling, it is unlikely to become a reality. However, the government may take some remedial measures, such as subsidizing exports and reducing import taxes. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

(Budapest) The Italian currency devaluation could have a major impact on Hungary, as Hungary exports a large number of goods to Italy and is therefore a creditor to Italy. After the lira devaluation, the clearing business between Italy and Hungary has automatically stopped, and as a result, Italy's purchases from Hungary will inevitably decrease. Political figures here believe that although the Italian government has stated that it must maintain trade with Hungary and promote its development, if the currency devaluation measures have a negative impact on Hungary, then Hungary will have to turn to Germany and try to develop trade as a means of damage control. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

(New York) US Senator Pittman, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, recently issued a statement saying, "The signing of the currency agreement between the United Kingdom, France, and the United States is the greatest achievement of President Roosevelt's tenure. After the signing of this agreement, there is no need to pass new laws in Congress." Pittman also said that when the London Conference was held in 1933, it was not possible to stabilize the exchange rates of various currencies, because the United Kingdom was unwilling to raise the exchange rate of the pound, and France also refused to devalue the franc. Therefore, the general atmosphere was very unfavorable. The Republican Party used this to accuse President Roosevelt, saying that Roosevelt was primarily responsible for the failure of the London Economic Conference, which can be said to be extremely unfair. Even according to the estimate of Harrison of the Federal Reserve Bank of New York, it was impossible to stabilize the currencies of various countries at that time. (Havas News Agency, 5th)

(Washington) Government officials expressed their views today, saying that the Italian currency devaluation can enhance the effectiveness of the currency agreement between the United Kingdom, France, and the United States. Generally speaking, this move can be regarded as another step towards restoring international currency values to the proportions in the early post-war period. (National News Agency, 5th)

Valuable metals stored by the people should also be deposited in banks to replenish the national treasury. In addition, all residents of the city must be prepared for rebel air raids. British Labour Party Congress Supports Neutral Policy on Spanish Civil War

(Edinburgh) The Labour Party Congress today passed a resolution supporting the government's non-interference policy in the Spanish Civil War by a majority of 1,836,000 votes to 519,000 votes. There was a lengthy debate before the vote. Greenwood, Secretary of the Labour Party's Information Department, told the delegates that this policy had been acknowledged as the responsibility of the leader of the French Popular Front government, Léon Blum. The initiator of this policy was the Blum government, and it was endorsed by Soviet Russia. At present, all European public opinion, whether socialist or non-socialist, recognizes the non-interference policy as a genuine way out in an extremely serious situation. At the opening of the Labour Party Congress, the riots that occurred in London yesterday immediately aroused repercussions. Morrison, former chairman of the Labour Party Congress, put forward a resolution requesting the government to immediately investigate the recent riots and the activities and financial resources of the British fascist organizations. The entire meeting unanimously passed the resolution. Discussions on the government's rearmament policy will begin in the near future. The national defense proposal that has been included in the agenda contains the following: "The Congress, in view of the threatening attitude of autocratic countries around the world, which are massively increasing their armaments, disregarding international law, and refusing to join the work of organizing peace, hereby declares that the military strength of the countries of the League of Nations must be determined by the military strength of the aggressors. The Congress hereby reaffirms that the Labour Party's policy of maintaining national defense is in line with the responsibilities that member states of the League of Nations should bear. Its purpose is to preserve the rights and freedoms of the people, uphold democracy, and abide by international law. The Labour Party recognizes the relationship between foreign policy and armaments and believes that the government's past performance is extremely pitiful. Therefore, it expresses its refusal to take responsibility for a purely competitive armaments policy. The Congress reserves its complete freedom to criticize the current government's rearmament and believes that continued investment in private arms manufacturing is a major threat to world peace." (Reuters News Agency, 5th)

Ministry of Finance: Land Transportation Inspection Office Moved to Tianjin; Branch Office Established in Datong to Intercept Smuggled Goods; Customs Commissioners of Tianjin and Qinhuangdao Changed

(Tianjin Communication) The anti-smuggling measures in North China have not yet been finalized. Li Tong, Deputy Director of the Land Transportation Inspection Office, is still in Tianjin awaiting orders from the Ministry of Finance after coming to North China to investigate. Whether the General Inspection Office will move north is expected to be decided clearly by the central government within the next week. According to Li Tong's interviews with various authorities in North China and responsible persons of the Tianjin Customs, he summarized the opinions of all parties and believed that with the establishment of inspection branch offices in various places, smugglers have found it difficult to transport goods, and the amount of smuggled goods has gradually decreased. However, the environment in Tianjin is special, and the puppet regime in Eastern Hebei has not been abolished for a while. Smuggled goods have thus taken Tianjin as their source and are being forcibly sold to the hinterland of Hebei and Chahar. In September, the total value of goods sold was 2,025,000 yuan, including 66,000 bags of sugar, 5,000 boxes of rayon, 5,000 boxes of kerosene, 3,000 boxes of wool fabrics, and 4,500 pieces of miscellaneous marine goods. The amount is truly staggering. Although there are customs three-point checkpoints in the suburbs of Tianjin, originally intended to take a sealing-off approach and prevent smuggled goods from being transported out of Tianjin, since their establishment, in addition to increasing the customs' financial burden, they have not achieved any effect. Japanese smugglers all use military trucks with heavy loads, insert the Japanese flag, and break through the tax checkpoints, refusing to listen to any obstruction or inspection. Although the Tianjin municipal police have come out to assist, there is no way to deal with the Japanese smugglers who are armed and difficult to deal with. Forcibly executing the law will inevitably lead to a bloody tragedy. Therefore, customs officers are becoming increasingly timid, and smuggling is becoming more rampant and unscrupulous. The private goods on the Ping-Sui Railway have, in the past month, because of the completion of the Zhang-Duo Highway, all abandoned the method of using the railway for transportation and switched to loading long-distance buses, starting from Rehe and transferring to the Northwest along the Zhang-Duo Highway. Daily necessities with surprisingly cheap prices have been found in Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, and western Suiyuan provinces. Only because transportation in that area is difficult, the sales market has not been smooth. Based on this situation, Li Tong telegraphed to the central government, with an accompanying suggestion, requesting that the General Inspection Office be moved to Tianjin first. Although it will not be possible to eliminate the source and completely eliminate the path of smuggling, it is undeniable that smugglers take Tianjin as their base camp. At present, smuggling in Jiangnan is no longer rampant, only smuggling in Hebei is still the same. If the source of smuggled goods in Tianjin is blocked, then although smuggling cannot be completely eliminated for a while, it can be gradually reduced due to inconvenient sales. In addition, since there is no private goods transportation on the Ping-Sui Railway, the establishment of a branch office can be eliminated. However, since they have been found in Gansu, Suiyuan, Qinghai, and Ningxia, in addition to ordering the authorities of each province to strictly prevent and block them, another inspection branch office should be established in Datong to replace the former Changguan and intercept smuggled goods from invading and selling. If all places outside Hebei Province can adopt the form of a large encirclement and strictly block them, the General Inspection Office can be moved to Tianjin to assist the customs in removing the roots of private traffickers and gradually reduce the sales channels of smuggled goods. Given a reasonable amount of time, it may be possible to eradicate them completely. It is heard that the Ministry of Finance quite agrees, and the movement of the General Office to Tianjin may become a reality. In the future, An Sier will come to Tianjin to preside over everything, and Li Tong will be stationed in Tianjin for a long time, coordinating the affairs of the Ping-Han and Jin-Pu branch offices.

As for the work of the Inspection Office, it has generally been decided internally, and it will be implemented after the official order is issued. As for the Tianjin and Qinhuangdao customs themselves, the Ministry of Finance has repeatedly received reports that Customs Commissioner Xu Liya of Tianjin Customs and Customs Commissioner Morley of Qinhuangdao Customs are unsuitable for the place and are also mostly perfunctory in their work. In order to improve the organization of the customs themselves and strengthen their external strength, Mei Weiliang, Customs Commissioner of the Jianghan Customs, and Dukes, Customs Commissioner of the Wenzhou Customs, were specially transferred to serve as Customs Commissioners of the Tianjin and Qinhuangdao Customs, respectively. Mei Weiliang arrived in Tianjin on the 4th and took over on the 5th. Dukes will arrive in Qinhuangdao around the 10th to take office. After the two customs are reorganized by the Ministry of Finance, they will jointly assume responsibility with the General Inspection Office, and there should be thorough measures to suppress smuggling. The inspection offices set up in Hebei and Chahar were previously discussed by Li Qingxuan when he came to the north, and they should specialize in suppressing military fire, drugs, and bandits, and they must follow this route. There is no conflict with the authority of the customs. Gu Cun's supplemental tax on smuggled goods in Tianjin established a committee to be responsible for investigation and liquidation. Although Li Qingxuan has reported to the Ministry of Finance, how the supplemental tax rate should be stipulated is also a matter of great research. Because the authorities of Hebei and Chahar had said in advance that they would allow the Japanese to pay 1/8 of the regular customs tax, the Ministry of Finance intends to believe that it is already showing generosity to let them pay the full regular tax rate and release the goods without investigating the crime of smuggling. If it is lower than the customs tax rate, it is absolutely impossible. Therefore, the establishment of this meeting is still in doubt. (5th)

Overseas Chinese in Vladivostok Expelled and Returned to China; Refugees Talk About the Cruel Circumstances of Their Expulsion

(Qingdao Communication) In recent years, our overseas Chinese compatriots have been expelled and returned to the country due to the exclusion of foreign ethnic groups. Now, the Chinese compatriots living in Vladivostok have been expelled and returned to the country. More than a dozen refugees, all over the age of 50, who arrived in Qingdao by ship from Yantai yesterday, the oldest of whom was named Yu Peicai, aged 75, wandered the streets after arriving in Qingdao because they were unfamiliar with the place and no one took them in, which was extremely pitiful. After being spotted by police officers from the 10th Police Station of the 1st Public Security Bureau, they were immediately brought to the station for questioning and learned that they were Chinese compatriots who had been expelled from Vladivostok. They were sent to the Taihe Inn on Tai'an Road to spend the night and promised to ask the Social Affairs Bureau for relief on their behalf. According to them, the circumstances of their expulsion were extremely cruel. I will now record the refugees' talks. I went to Guandong 20 years ago to make a living. At that time, it was the most popular thing for people from Shandong. Young people in general were eager to cross the north. Indeed, those who went to Guandong at that time were very rich. When we went, we were all around 20 years old, and we always sent home two or three hundred yuan every year. Unexpectedly, after the September 18th Incident, we could no longer survive. All kinds of donations, taxes, and insurances were really a hassle. That's not all. The most deadly thing is that you are given a crime for no reason. Lightly, you will be put in a big prison, and heavily, you will be shot. Originally, you could earn about one yuan a day, but after the incident, it was reduced to less than 30 cents. After paying the donations and taxes, you simply didn't have enough to eat. Because there was no way, we transferred to Vladivostok in Russia. When we first arrived, it was easy to earn money, and we could earn two or three yuan a day. Later, I heard that it was occupied by some party, and the treatment of overseas Chinese was extremely cruel. We were simply put in a prison again. Not only was the salary reduced by more than half, but the money earned had to be spent on the same day, and no extra money was allowed. When we go out to make a living, who doesn't have parents, wives, and children at home? Who doesn't want to save a few dollars to take home? It's strange that as long as you have a line, they will definitely find it, and the result is a big prison. They can arbitrarily stipulate ten or twenty years. Therefore, there are no less than hundreds of thousands of Chinese people in Vladivostok who are in prison. This is not a big deal. Since this spring, they don't want Chinese people at all. When you are working, they will grab your ear and tell you to leave. No money or luggage is allowed to be carried. Every day, there must be thousands of Chinese people who suddenly become homeless. It's really pitiful. Fortunately, we have a consul there, so we can find a way to send us back. Originally, we should have passed through the three northeastern provinces to return to the country, but the laws stipulated by the puppet state are very strict. If we pass through that place without a passport, we will be shot if we are caught. Therefore, the consul told us to go from Vladivostok to Shanghai. There are two decisions every month. Each decision can transport more than 500 people. Now, no less than tens of thousands of people have been expelled and returned to the country. After we arrived in Shanghai, because we are from Shandong, the Shanghai Public Security Bureau sent us by ship to Yantai. There were more than 50 people who arrived in Yantai this time. Because we are very close to Qingdao, the Yantai Red Swastika Society sent us on the Maoli ship. We arrived in Qingdao at 3 pm today (the 4th). We ate a full meal at the Yantai Red Swastika Society yesterday, and we haven't eaten since. He couldn't help but sigh.

Pine River: Fellow Tradesmen Violently Chopped with Axes

Wu Changchu, a Wuxi native, 31 years old, was a partner in the Qiande Tai carpentry shop west of Xiuye Bridge. Previously, because the industry guild and the county middle school were connected, the school expanded its campus, exchanging land in another place with the industry and adding 240 yuan. It was unexpected that this money would be used privately. Wu Changchu had submitted a report to the county government, requesting a thorough investigation and recovery, which caused resentment from those who divided the money. They repeatedly hinted to Wu that if he did not stop submitting and urging, he would be in trouble. Unexpectedly, at around 10 pm last night (the 5th), Wu Changchu was returning to the store from east to west when several people flashed out of the Dongbaidu Lane. They chopped Wu's head, shoulders, and back with axes. The axe on the back of his head caused the most serious injury. Wu recognized that they were his fellow tradesmen Du Jiangying, Xie Aquan, Chun Gen, Yang, and five others whose names he did not know. Seeing that Wu was injured, they immediately fled. Passers-by informed Wu Changchu's store to send someone to carry him to Joseph Hospital for treatment. It is heard that the perpetrators have now asked someone to come forward to mediate, but the local public security police station is still investigating the perpetrators.

Kunshan: Male Corpse Found Strangled

On the morning of the 5th, an unidentified male corpse was found in the river west of Han Bridge, No. 90 Hukun Highway near Qingyang Port in the county. He was about 30 years old. The villagers discovered and reported to the police district, and telegraphed the county government to send someone to examine the body. The male corpse had a white belt tied around his neck. The skin color of his whole body was pale white, his eyes were closed, and water was seeping from his nostrils. There were scars on his right foot and back. It was obvious that he had been strangled to death before being pushed into the river. The corpse was ordered to be collected by the Baolizhang first, and the murderer was strictly arrested to be dealt with according to the law.

Taicang: The Heroic Act of Strong Men Dredging the River

The original Yicang River inside the Xiaobeimen of this city has been desolate for many years and has become a flat land. However, because this area is the district where the county's organs are concentrated, fire protection is particularly inconvenient. The county government has prepared a plan for the strong men of the first district to be responsible for dredging. From the 5th to the 7th, the work was completed. The strong men worked bravely and were not afraid of hardship, which is a heroic act.

Suzhou: Year of Abundance Reports Sounds of Famine

This year's harvest is abundant, unseen in many years. However, due to wind and insect disasters in a small number of rural areas, reports of famine have been submitted to the county. The county government has instructed Yan Hongsheng, the accounting director of Wujiang, to conduct on-site inspections in Xiangcheng Weiting and other areas on the 4th and 5th. The results show that the losses in the above two areas are minimal, and in some cases, the disaster-stricken areas cannot be identified. Yesterday (the 6th), Commissioner Yan went to the Mu Hu Guan and other areas for inspection, which is expected to be completed today (the 7th). The situation will be reported to the Finance Department to determine the quality of the autumn harvest. Deng Jie, the accounting director of Wu County, went to Wujiang for inspection on the 6th. Furthermore, in the Chefang area, the early rice harvest is about 80%, while the late rice has suffered more severely due to the devastation of heavy fog, wind, rain, and extreme heat. The area has already reported to the county and requested a joint inspection with the owners to determine the quality.

Wuxi: Stout Men's Team Maintains Winter Defense

The First District Office, following the county's promulgated "Elimination Measures," emphasizes stout men's patrols. With the winter defense period approaching, the office plans to organize the trained stout men in the district into a stout men's team to maintain local security. This was proposed for discussion at yesterday's district affairs meeting. It was unanimously agreed that maintaining local security starts with eliminating scattered bandits. Township heads should consider the local situation and distribute the number of stout men according to the promulgated measures. At the same time, opinions should be added to the organization of self-defense groups and reported to the district office for approval.

Gloomy Future for the Silk Market

This year's autumn cocoon harvest is extremely poor in both Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and the silk reeling is also inferior to that of the spring cocoons. However, due to the small output, the price of cocoons has risen, exceeding the prescribed purchase price by nearly ten yuan. Therefore, cocoon merchants are deeply concerned about the risk of losses, and the money industry is also advocating caution regarding loan collateral. Weighing is now uniformly carried out everywhere. Recently, international trade in Chinese silk has been affected by the dumping of Japanese silk, resulting in a sharp decline in transactions and a sharp drop in prices. B-grade standard silk has fallen to 600 yuan upon entering customs. Domestic silk factories, due to the current situation, dare not purchase it. As a result, silk sales are extremely sluggish, and the market outlook is very bleak.

Changshu: Malignant Malaria Prevalent in Various Townships

Since the beginning of autumn, a type of malignant malaria has been prevalent in various townships in Muyi. It is even more widespread in the eastern townships. According to Chinese medicine diagnoses, it is typhoid fever. In the various townships of the Sixth District, sufferers are everywhere, and the situation is quite severe. Many patients die without being saved. The duration of the illness is often five or six days, and some die in as little as two or three days. When they first fall ill, patients can still sit up, but when it becomes severe, it is impossible to save them.

Jiangyin: Order from the Department to Dismantle and Reduce the Coal Wharf

The Jingjiang County Party Headquarters reported that the Zhongxing Coal Wharf in Huangtiangang Port, Jiangyin, protrudes into the river, forcing the water flow to the north, and the embankment on the north bank is collapsing severely. The Construction Department sent engineer Zhou Kebao to Cheng the day before yesterday to conduct an on-site inspection with local officials from Jiangyin and Jingjiang counties. Upon returning to the province, he reported that the wharf's impact on changing the river flow was small, but it was prone to silting, which had a significant impact. Based on the report, the Construction Department ordered the Jiangyin County Magistrate to independently implement the dismantling and reduction and report it for verification.

Huaiyin: Traveler Brutally Kills Innkeeper

Zhou Qian, who runs the Changfa Inn outside the North Wei Gate in Wangying Town, the Third District of this county, was suddenly approached by five unfamiliar strangers on the evening of the 2nd, who claimed to be lodging. To their surprise, in the middle of the night, Zhou Qian was suddenly hacked in the chest with an axe, suffering serious injuries and dying. Two of the five lodgers escaped, and the other three also left one after another. Zhou Qian's daughter, upon discovering the incident, immediately reported it to the township office. On the morning of the 3rd, District Chief Shi Dongshan went to investigate and immediately reported it to the county government to send personnel to conduct an autopsy. The autopsy revealed that Zhou Qian's left ear, left face, and brain were all hacked open, with blood splattered everywhere. The scene was extremely tragic. However, the identity of the murderer is currently difficult to determine.

Gaoyou: Abduction of Bride Results in Tragedy

Hu Xiulai, a resident of the northern township of the Seventh District of this county, had a second daughter named Er Guniang, who was twenty years old. She had been betrothed to the son of Hao Sanmao in her childhood. Hao's son had been serving in the military for many years with no news. This spring, Hu decided to marry his daughter to the son of Li Dapei, a wealthy merchant in Lingzhen, and the wedding was imminent. Unexpectedly, Hao's son returned home the day before yesterday and learned that his fiancée had been betrothed to someone else and the wedding was about to take place. On the evening of the 2nd, Hao's son gathered a group of people and went to his future in-laws' house by boat to abduct the bride. After successfully getting the girl back on the boat, Hu sounded the alarm, and villagers gathered and rushed to the Xiaoyang Port where the boat was docked. They rescued Hu's daughter. Hao's son and his men were outnumbered and the boat sank into the lake. Li San drowned because he did not know how to swim. On the morning of the 3rd, the incident was reported to the Fifth Police Substation, and Hao's son was arrested. A formal lawsuit has been filed.

Taizhou: Notorious Bandit in the Southern District Executed

Ye Zhikun, a notorious bandit in the southern district of Wenling, was 44 years old. He surrendered and reformed in 1931, but later re-formed a gang, gathered at sea, and robbed merchant ships. He was subsequently arrested by the local defense team and escorted to the county government. After a thorough interrogation and confirmation of the facts, he was sentenced to death according to law. After approval from higher authorities, a team was dispatched to Songmen Town in the southern district at 8:00 AM on the 2nd to carry out the execution by firing squad as a warning.

Hangzhou: Major Accident on the Hanghui Road

The Hangtun Intermodal Passenger Bus on the Hanghui Highway left Hangzhou for Tunxi at 7:00 AM yesterday. When it reached the Linxia Village area of Changhua County, a nearby farmer named Chen, who was over 50 years old, was walking on the highway and was unable to avoid the bus. He was knocked down and seriously injured by the car. He was sent to the county hospital for treatment, but died at 4:00 PM. Also, the Hangwei Company's #2135 freight car, which was carrying soldiers from She County to Changhua to suppress bandits, fell from a mountain ridge that was five or six stories high in the Yuling Pass area at 4:00 PM this afternoon due to the driver's negligence. Two people died instantly, and seventeen people were seriously injured. The driver was also injured and is currently being treated at the Hangzhou Municipal Hospital.

Bengbu: Reducing the Salt Tax in Sanhejian

The Henan Sales and Tax Bureau reported to the Ministry of Finance that the Sanhejian area is adjacent to the low-tax area of northern Anhui, which is prone to smuggling. It proposed to reduce the sales tax on Huai salt transported by river in the area by one yuan per dan and reduce the sales tax on salt carried by shoulder by nine jiao per dan for a six-month trial period to increase sales and enrich tax revenue. The Ministry of Finance approved the report and ordered the General Inspectorate to inform the Lianghuai Salt Transport Envoy. The Bengbu Tax Collection Office has received this clear order.

European Tour - Letter

Chen Jitang and Hu Wenhu

— Xu Shu

The ship arrived in Hong Kong and then departed. There were many people seeing it off at the pier, with red and green paper streamers hanging all along the ship's railing. From here to Singapore is a journey of three days and one night, starting at 4:00 PM on August 30th.

Two more famous Chinese figures boarded the ship's first-class cabin: Chen Jitang and Hu Wenhu. The former is a defeated hero, taking a lot of money abroad; the latter is a successful wealthy man, returning to his old home in Singapore. I have some inexplicable feelings about these two famous people.

The day before arriving in Singapore, the students had a gathering. Someone suggested that when in Singapore, they should invite Mr. Hu Wenhu to give some guidance and to extend some hospitality, and also visit his businesses in Singapore. To be honest, these newly fledged Chinese children wanted to squeeze some money out of this overseas Chinese millionaire who is very enthusiastic about everything in China. They also wanted to get to know this great man whose industries are declining but whose evergreen spirit remains.

News of the meeting reached the first-class cabin. I heard that General Chen suspected it was a meeting against him or something, and felt very uneasy, sending people to inquire from all sides. This hero, who was invincible in Guangzhou, felt fear at a meeting of fifty students on this white ship. This kind of mentality is something we cannot understand, nor can our compatriots in the country understand, I think.

The procedure for contacting Mr. Hu Wenhu was to write him a letter first, but after waiting for two days without a reply, they had to send a representative to see him. However, Mr. Hu Wenhu was very cold, first saying that there was nothing to do in Singapore, and second that time was tight and he could not entertain them. Anyway, he didn't know how to say it. Mr. Hu only speaks Cantonese, and we could only communicate with him through a Cantonese dialect speaker. As a result, he said that if it wasn't too much trouble, he might send a clerk and a large car to accompany and guide them when possible.

However, Singapore arrived at 6:00 AM the next day, and until 9:00 AM, neither the clerk nor the car came. Nothing was very certain, so who would patiently wait for an unreliable opportunity?

We took a car to the Botanical Garden. Because there was no prior organization and there were many people, things were not well arranged. We went to the museum in a hurry. The museum was originally named Raffles Library. Sir Thomas Stamford Raffles was the first builder of Singapore. This museum has a bit of a memorial character to him, so there is a statue of him at the entrance.

The museum has a wide collection of things. The history and culture of the Malay people, and other valuable equipment and utensils, are displayed in a very complete way. Malay culture is very similar to Chinese culture in many ways. We can compare many things. Ships and weapons were very developed early on. The carvings on the sword handles and the production of many metal inlays were perfected very early on. However, their people, those who are slightly knowledgeable and advanced, have become Europeanized, and there is no longer any Eastern personality.

After leaving the museum, we took rickshaws to eat. Rickshaws here can seat two people. I sat in one with Professor Zhao Renqiao from Tsinghua University. Although Mr. Zhao is a bit fat, I am thin, but even with both of us sitting down, it still felt too narrow. I thought this might be specially designed for a man and a woman to sit together.

The majority of people wanted to eat Chinese food. They hadn't eaten Chinese food for five days, and they all wanted to eat it. As for me, I didn't need it yet. First, because many people treated me to meals when I left, the aftertaste hadn't faded. Second, because I am used to living in the north and love to eat wheat-based foods. I am afraid that the only restaurants here are Cantonese restaurants, and I am most afraid of Cantonese food, so I didn't feel any interest.

Singapore's currency is half more expensive than Hong Kong's, and naturally even more expensive than Shanghai's. Although there were many of us, we didn't drink alcohol or choose expensive dishes, but it still cost more than fourteen yuan. Fourteen yuan is close to thirty yuan in Shanghai money, which would be enough to eat a good meal in Shanghai. —Thinking like this, it's no wonder that Mr. Hu Wenhu was unwilling to treat us.

When we went there, we took a car, passing through many streets, and also passed Mr. Hu Wenhu's home. Mr. Hu's home is a very nice Western-style house, but the inside and outside of the gate are decorated with several large and small stone-made colorful tigers and leopards made of cement. The name Hu Wenhu is engraved under the tiger, and the name Hu Wenbao is engraved under the leopard, making them even more eye-catching. The billboards on the street are all Tiger Balm tiger trademarks. Occasionally, a car would pass by, with a tiger standing on the roof and advertisements on the car cover. This shows Mr. Hu Wenhu's status in Singapore.

According to people who know, Mr. Hu is an overseas Chinese who has been making and selling Chinese secret recipes in the tropics for generations. When the rubber tree industry was booming, many people seized the opportunity, but Mr. Hu was not moved at all and still wholeheartedly devoted himself to the Tiger Balm business. Year after year, at a time when many rubber industry operators were going bankrupt, he showed even greater financial strength.

Walking back from the street, I felt an unspeakable emotion about Singapore's clean municipality. All of this Europeanized architecture and layout has long lost the elegant and exquisite Eastern culture of the Malay people in the museum. The only remnants on this island under British rule, which can be said to be a symbol of Eastern culture, are the simple colorful tigers and leopards on the walls of Mr. Hu Wenhu's residence, company cars, and signboards. I had met Mr. Hu Wenhu on the ship. This robust, well-dressed wealthy businessman is trying to preserve this Chinese Dragon Boat Festival trademark, which is indeed not easy.

Under the economic strategies of imperialism here, only Mr. Hu still exists unyieldingly, which is already an amazing feat. But Tiger Balm can only be sold among the Chinese, Malays, and Indians. What other feelings do I have about this outstanding wealthy businessman? The piers are full of small stalls selling shirts, pants, socks, and other items from Chinese hawkers, while the warships of the great British Empire stand tall in the harbor. Heavens, what time is it? It is already dusk. Leaning on the railing of the white Italian ship, I couldn't help but think of my distant homeland. But then I immediately thought, after Mr. Hu Wenhu went ashore, in the grand and magnificent first-class cabin salon, I am afraid that there would only be three or four Chinese people including General Chen, right? They sit on the deck, looking out the window, what kind of feelings will they have about this poor and backward homeland? (September 8, 1936, on the Indian Ocean).

Page 8

Educational News

National Boy Scout Grand Review to Open Tomorrow Morning: President Chiang Inspects Camp, Confirms Schedule, and Announces Awards, Over Four Hundred Items Received, Sixteen Units Reported

Nanjing, 6th: By the 6th, over four hundred awards flags, silver shields, and inscribed plaques donated from various parties for the Boy Scout Grand Review have been received. These include Chairman Lin's "Valuing Martiality and Unity," President Chiang's "Accumulating Strength for Heroism," Vice President He Yingqin's "Martiality and Health Exceeding the Ordinary," President Ju's "Martial Spirit," Commander-in-Chief Lu's "Upholding Our Martial Virtue," President Yu's "Brand New Barriers," and President Sun's "Sincere Vigour," which are sufficient to boost national prestige and encourage the masses.

Nanjing, 6th: President Chiang arrived in the suburbs of Nanjing from Jiangxi on the 5th to review the Boy Scout encampment for the Grand Review. He first made a low-altitude flight over the camp, leaning against the aircraft window to conduct a detailed inspection. The sound of military aircraft whirring in the field and the sight of the President sitting upright inside the aircraft caused everyone to stand at attention and pay their respects. The aircraft circled once before descending to the city and landing. Vice President He Yingqin went to the camp this morning to inspect the arrangements in various districts, and Grand Assembly Advisor Ma Chaojun also went to inspect.

Nanjing, 6th: As of the evening of the 6th, the following sixteen units have reported for the National Boy Scout Grand Review: Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Beijing, Anhui, Hebei, Fujian, Henan, Hunan, Tianjin, Shaanxi, Hubei, Guizhou, Gansu, Chahar, Shanghai, and Ningbo. Jiangsu is led by Chen Bang扌, with 3131 service personnel and male and female Scouts. Beijing is led by Zhou Bomin, with a total of 1067 service personnel and Scouts. Anhui has Xu Min and others with 608 people. Hebei has Li Daoming and others with 447 people. Fujian has Liu Xuezhao and others with 273 people. Henan has Zhou Youguang and others with 294 people. Hunan has Qiu Shuofu and others with 181 people. Tianjin has Ren Shuyuan and others with 199 people. Shaanxi has Peng Zhenhuan and others with 122 people. Hubei has Chen Lesan and others with 124 people. Guizhou has He Jianheng and others with 21 people. Gansu has Mao Shengzu and others with 10 people. Chahar has Zhang Guohua and others with 28 people. Zhejiang is led by Xu Shaodi. Shanghai Jiangning has already sent service personnel to the camp to provide service. There are also units from Shanxi, Guangdong, Yunnan, Suiyuan, and Guangzhou that have not reported to the camp management team. It is expected that a total of twenty-eight units will participate. In terms of awards, there is a silver tower from Committee Chairman Chiang, silver tripods from President and Vice Presidents Dai and He, and various awards from other officials, which are displayed at the Preparatory Committee office in a magnificent manner.

The First National Grand Review and Encampment of the Boy Scouts of China will open in Beijing tomorrow (the 8th) at 6:00 AM. The finally confirmed schedule is as follows:

From the 3rd to the 7th, registration and encampment will be handled, registration for various activities will take place, and application forms will be issued. The location is the Preparatory Committee Office inside the new Lingyuan Village Grand Encampment Camp. Registration will begin on October 3rd and end on the 7th.

From 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM on the 7th, a meeting of the General Leaders will be convened. The location will be announced temporarily, and the time may be extended if necessary. Also, from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM, there will be a movie. The location will be announced temporarily.

From 6:00 AM to 7:00 AM on the 8th, there will be an opening ceremony. The location is the camp. Each unit will gather in its respective camp area. Also, from 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM, there will be a review rehearsal at the Central Stadium. From 1:30 PM to 5:30 PM, there will be labour service in the city of Nanjing for the male Scouts and in the villages near Lingyuan for the female Scouts. Also, from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM, the camp will be open for public viewing. The time may be temporarily announced to be stopped if necessary. Bonfire parties will be held in the football field and at the National Martial Arts College in separate areas.

From 8:00 AM to 11:30 AM on the 9th, there will be a review rehearsal at the Central Stadium. From 1:30 PM to 5:30 PM, there will be an air defense drill at the football field. The camp will be open for public viewing. Also, from 7:30 PM to 9:00 PM, there will be an air defense drill at the camp.

From 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM on the 10th, there will be a National Day commemoration and review ceremony at the Central Stadium. The time may be temporarily changed if necessary. Also, from 8:00 AM to 5:30 PM, the camp will be open for public viewing. Also, from 2:00 PM to 6:00 PM, there will be course performances held in separate areas. Also, from 7:30 PM to 9:00 PM, there will be a lantern parade in the city of Nanjing. The time may be extended if necessary.

From 8:00 AM to 9:00 AM on the 11th, there will be a memorial service for the death of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and a closing ceremony at the mausoleum. At 9:00 AM, the dismantling of the camp will begin. (1) The Boy Scout artwork exhibition will be held at the Revolutionary Memorial Hall in Linggu Temple. The visiting hours will be determined separately. (2) The Boy Scout affairs discussion meeting will be convened temporarily after the end of the Grand Assembly. (3) If there are any changes to the schedule, the Preparatory Committee will revise and announce them at any time.

Wang Shijie Cables Dai Chuanxian to Return to Beijing to Participate in the Boy Scout Grand Review

Nanjing, 6th: Dai Chuanxian arrived in Hong Kong on the 6th and entered Guangdong. It is reported that Dean Wang cabled Dai on the 6th, urging him to rush to participate in the Boy Scout Grand Review before the scheduled date.

This City's Boy Scouts Went to Beijing Last Night to Participate

According to Guomin News Agency, the Second National Boy Scout Grand Encampment and Grand Review will open tomorrow morning at the Lingyuan in Beijing. This city's Boy Scouts and service personnel, a total of eight or nine hundred people, gathered in military uniform at the North Station at around 6:00 PM last night. The General Leader Shen Tongyi called the roll and organized the team. More than a thousand students from the Aesthetic Society, Rotary Club, and more than ten other schools arrived at the station to line up and see them off. At 8:00 PM, a flag-presenting ceremony was held on the platform. After the ceremony was carried out, Mr. Shao Rugan, on behalf of Mayor Wu and Director Pan, presented the flag and gave an impromptu speech with many words of encouragement, which moved the listeners. The ceremony ended at 9:00 PM, and the entire group boarded the train and departed for Beijing. It is reported that the entire team is scheduled to return to Shanghai on the 13th. In addition, more than forty members of the Kuangyi Boy Scout Corps, who were all selected as representatives of this city to attend the National Review, also went to Beijing last night. Disturbance Occurs at Chuzhong, Two Classes of Students Leave School, Situation Further Escalates

The Zhejiang Provincial Chuzhou Junior High School held a Boy Scout group this semester. For the sake of uniform attire, on September 30th, tailors were ordered to measure and make woolen overcoats (at a price of more than ten yuan each). The third-year students, because they were about to graduate soon and had already made cotton overcoats last year, politely requested to be exempted from measurement in order to save money and reduce the burden on their parents and elders. Principal Zhao Zhongsu then forcibly imposed sanctions and said that anyone who dared to resist would be expelled. Soon, the entire class of third-year students also opposed this matter and left the school entirely at around 5:00 PM on October 1st. Principal Zhao immediately identified the initiating student, Chen Faxiang, and threatened him with beatings, ordering him to reveal the names of his accomplices and ordering the students to leave the school immediately. Chen Faxiang was also taken to the Public Security Bureau by the police and detained. On the morning of the 2nd, the entire class of first-year students also left the school. The situation has further escalated, and mediation by the local authorities is quite difficult.
