Swiss Philanthropist Enthusiastically Assists with Donations

Mrs. Nobel of Switzerland has always been enthusiastic about international charitable causes. Recently, she came to China with her husband for business and witnessed the large number of disaster victims in our country and the hardship of their lives. Her compassion arose spontaneously. Upon learning that the China International Famine Relief Commission at 505 Henan Road in this city is a well-known relief organization in our country, she personally visited to learn about the general situation of their work and expressed great sympathy. She immediately donated five yuan in national currency and expressed her willingness to undertake voluntary publicity. She then wrote an article about the disaster situation in our country and published it in the International Gazette and various newspapers in Geneva, widely soliciting donations to aid the relief effort. Many people were moved by her and generously donated to the cause. According to the person in charge of the Relief Commission, they have recently received many donations from Switzerland. Although the amounts are not large, the sincerity is very sincere. One donor, who signed as "Swiss Mother," sent one gold yuan and wrote in a letter that her financial resources were meager and she could not donate much money. Given the severity of the disaster situation in your country, she was doing her best to fulfill her responsibility of mutual assistance with her savings. Another donor, Ms. Doron, remitted a donation of eight shillings, stating that no receipt was needed to save on postage and to transfer the money to help the disaster victims. More recently, the Swiss Youth League collected donations from 30 people, totaling fifteen pounds and seven shillings, equivalent to 256.52 yuan in national currency, and remitted it to Mrs. Nobel for transmission to the Commission. The kindness of foreign philanthropists is truly touching.

The China Health Association, Which Promotes Health Insurance, Will Have a Joint Service Organization with Physicians and Hospitals Throughout the City.

Healthcare, or rather sickness insurance, has been practiced in various countries for a long time, with significant results in improving national health. Our country has never had such an organization. In light of the current social situation, this type of organization is becoming increasingly necessary. There are two reasons for this: (1) Due to the decline of the social economy and the difficulty of general life, neither individuals nor families can afford the burden of medical expenses, and they feel the pain of being unable to seek medical treatment and hospitalization, which directly leads to the loss of individual happiness and indirectly affects the health of the entire nation. (2) Based on the above situation, doctors and hospitals generally feel it is difficult to maintain operations, which directly deals a major blow to the spirit of doctors and hospitals serving society, and indirectly affects the development of medicine in a country. Therefore, to solve this serious problem in today's society, the only way is to unite the people, doctors, and hospitals and establish a strong healthcare organization. On the one hand, we can pool the economic strength of the masses to seek medical protection for the masses and improve the health of the nation. On the other hand, we can pool the medical equipment of doctors and hospitals and increase opportunities for joint service to the masses. This can not only solve the problems of doctors and hospitals themselves but also promote various medical and health construction projects in society and consolidate the foundation for the development of medicine. It is reported that the China Health Association, initiated by the Hongqiao Sanitarium and organized with joint service from physicians and hospitals throughout the city, is currently actively underway and will be established soon.

Cai Xiaobai's Law Office Moves

After returning from a weary life in the diplomatic world, lawyer Xiaobai previously established his law office at 542 Avenue Joffre in the French Concession, handling litigation, appeals, and non-litigation matters under the jurisdiction of courts at all levels. His business was quite prosperous. Recently, due to the original location being insufficient for office use, he specially moved to 70 Pushih Road (at the intersection of Route Tenant de St. Paul) on September 4th. The phone number is 80269. He continues to work as usual. The assisting lawyers include Chen Haisen and Fu Dehe. All affairs in the office are also assisted by his fiancée, Ms. Li Yaoying, a former clerk of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The order is well-maintained, and the business has a prosperous trend.

Customs Seizes Contraband

The results of the national customs' seizure of opium, morphine, and other prohibited items in the second quarter of the Republic of China in 1936 (April, May, and June) are as follows: foreign and native drugs totaled 4344.66 grams, opium paste totaled 592.8 grams, opium residue totaled 148.666 grams, opium ash totaled 870.544 grams, heroin and other substances totaled 15.73 grams, poppy seeds totaled 3 grams, and various drugs containing toxic substances were estimated to be worth 333.35 yuan in national currency.

Shen Bao National Products Special Issue

A Glimpse of Foreigners' Love for National Products

— Yan Maode

It has been more than ten years since the promotion of national products began, but the effectiveness achieved is still very small. Generally speaking, urban modern men and women, from head to toe, the things they need are all fascinated by foreign goods, taking the purchase of foreign goods as extravagance, and becoming good customers of foreign goods. This invisible poison, as Dr. Sun Yat-sen said, "This is even more powerful than using millions of soldiers to kill us."

Let us observe the people of various countries, their psychology of loving national products really makes us feel ashamed. For example, Japanese people, whether at home or abroad, are happy to use national products. Even small things such as chopsticks and thread are eager to buy domestic goods, so the people are rich and the country is strong.

German parents often teach their children, "Use German pens, German ink, and German paper, and do not take even a little bit from foreign goods to prevent our country's (Germany's) money from flowing abroad." This is specially written here, hoping that the modern men and women who are addicted to foreign goods will also be enlightened and wake up.

Glory of the National Products Industry: Wuzhou Establishes a New Ten-Story Building

— Yang Xinsheng

Recently, a ten-story building has been erected on the corner of Fuzhou Road and Henan Road in Shanghai. People passing by who suddenly see this building would initially think it is a large bank - or a grand building of a foreign company. Looking carefully at the writing on this building, they will realize that it is actually the new ten-story building built by Wuzhou Pharmaceutical Factory itself.

Wuzhou Pharmaceutical Factory is the leader of the new pharmaceutical industry in our country and the vanguard of the national products industry in our country. It is now able to build its own ten-story building, a high-rise reaching the clouds. Such a magnificent scene is a glory for the national products industry in our country and a manifestation of the progress of the real industry in our country!

In the past, Wuzhou Pharmaceutical Factory and its affiliated factories created various household medicines and hygiene products... improving the health of the people and benefiting society. These achievements are very obvious. Especially the contributions to industry and national defense, such as the successful domestic glycerin, which is even more worthy of our admiration.

As for the interior of the company's ten-story new building, it has been properly arranged. The two floors below are the business department, and the floors above are office rooms, famous doctors' clinics, and staff dormitories. In the middle of the third floor, there is also a memorial hall for Mr. Xiang Songmao, the former general manager of the company, designed by famous craftsmen from Peiping, solemn and magnificent, to commemorate Mr. Songmao's martyrdom.

This year's Double Ten Festival, the company's new building will hold a completion ceremony and the unveiling ceremony of the Xiang Memorial Hall, and at the same time hold a 30th anniversary celebration, inviting people from all walks of life to visit, and especially invite Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang to give a speech. The achievement of this great undertaking is bound to have an unprecedented and enthusiastic celebration at that time!

Word of Contribution

Economic Strength and Vitality

— Yang An

Mr. Wang Xiaolai recently stated at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's National Products Exhibition: "Using foreign goods destroys the nation's economic strength and extinguishes the nation's vitality." In other words, to increase the nation's economic strength and expand the nation's vitality, only promoting domestic goods can achieve this goal.

Let us think about it. For the past fifty years, China has been trading with foreign countries, with annual trade deficits amounting to tens of millions of yuan. This is like sucking marrow and extracting essence. The outflow of silver each year is countless, leading to an empty national treasury and withered livelihoods. The nation's economic strength has become extremely weak, and the nation's vitality has become even more stagnant. Day after day, the lamp runs out of oil, creating an unprecedented national crisis, giving those who seek to harm us ample power and handing them a weapon, which is equivalent to suicide. The failure of China's foreign trade and the habit of favoring foreign goods are extremely painful to speak of. We have often said that if the Chinese people do not awaken and extricate themselves, and only esteem foreign goods, in ten years at most, or five years at least, China will reach a point beyond repair. The nation's strength is depleted, and its vitality is exhausted. Such a nation and people, existing as if about to perish, what else is there to await but destruction?

The people of the nation should understand what kind of era this is. Knives are being sharpened, constantly seeking trouble, constantly thinking of how to destroy and humiliate us. If we remain unaware and only protect our personal lives and property, this is how a nation destined for destruction behaves, and it is not what should be expected of the Chinese people. We believe that the national crisis is so severe that a state of emergency has already begun. We, as citizens and various sectors of industry, commerce, and finance, must make earnest preparations in terms of both economic strength and vitality. How should we begin?

To increase economic strength, we should pay attention to three aspects: manpower, material resources, and financial resources. Manpower can be trained and learned. Financial resources should be fully prepared with currency to prevent capital from fleeing and the national treasury from becoming empty. In particular, the outflow of capital should be avoided. The preparation of material resources, adjusting consumption, reducing consumption, centralizing production, and improving production are all points that should be paid attention to at present. And the core should be promoting domestic goods and using domestic goods. This is a critical juncture for the people of the nation today, and we must not let it go.

To increase vitality, the expansion of vitality lies in the communication between urban and rural areas. We must transform the desolate and dying countryside into a vibrant and energetic place, and transform the falsely prosperous cities into places of substantial strength. This depends on the communication between manufactured goods and local products. We hope that the products of urban factories will find outlets in the interior, and the raw materials and local products produced in rural areas can be exported to adjust surpluses and deficits, so that the rural economy can become flexible and boost its purchasing power, and the nation's vitality will be cultivated as a result.

This is the preparation we should have in this state of emergency, and it is also the work we should do in the midst of a severe national crisis.

Mr. Xu Guqing Who Sets an Example in Promoting National Goods

— Preparing to be Successful

Mr. Xu Guqing, a member of the National Government, whose name was Shaozhen, courtesy name Guqing, a licentiate from Panyu County, Guangdong, who enjoyed reading military books, was assigned to Jiangnan with the qualification of an expectant Daotai. He was greatly trusted by Duanwuqiao, the Governor-General of Liangjiang. When establishing the Ninth Zhen New Army, he adopted the system of micro-soldiers. At that time, many scholars from literary academies joined the military service. He requested that Mr. Xu be the commander (i.e., the officers used were all graduates of military academies and possessed strong nationalistic ideas, such as Zhao Sheng, a martyr from Zhenjiang, and Bai Wenwei, an important figure in the party-state. At that time, they were all under his command, so the seeds of revolution spread very quickly). Mr. Xu trained his soldiers with the principle of "sharing joys and hardships." Seeing officers who were students returning from studying abroad wearing Western clothes, he often asked what country the raw materials were from and how much they cost. Although he did not explicitly state that buying foreign goods would lead to the outflow of rights and interests, his subordinates knew his intention, and thereafter they dared not use foreign goods again. The influence gradually permeated, and it became a common practice. During the Wuchang Uprising in 1911, Zhang Xun and Tieliang, who were hostile to the New Army, incited Governor-General Zhang Renjun to treat the Ninth Zhen with contempt, so their actions were inconvenient. During the uprising, they were defeated and retreated to Danyang due to a lack of supplies. After Suzhou was successively restored, Chen Yingshi and Cheng Xuelou, the two governors, discussed and gathered the troops of the various provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang to form a joint army to besiege Jinling, and they publicly elected Mr. Xu as the commander-in-chief. After the capture of Nanjing, he was reassigned as the Nanjing Garrison Commander. Later, he followed the Premier to Guangdong and served in various important positions, maintaining integrity and self-discipline. After serving as a member of the National Government, he moved to Shanghai due to old age and illness. Although he was unable to walk well, he remained unremitting in promoting national goods. He specially made a car with a door opening in the back and a small two-wheeled cart like a child's to facilitate going out. In the Penglai City market, there were often traces of him leading his family to select and purchase national goods for household use. When Shanghai held national products exhibitions, he always went to visit. Last year, when a national products exhibition was held on the open space opposite the Great World, I had a long conversation with him. He said that promoting national goods is indeed a crucial plan to save the country, more important than any other work, because money is like blood in a person's body, and if it constantly flows out, how can the nation not be poor and weak and die young? National goods manufacturers should also research and improve the manufacturing aspect, so that they can compete with foreign goods. The common people, with the nature of loving beauty, cannot be forced not to buy foreign goods solely with the two words "patriotism." While speaking, he pointed to the clothes he was wearing and said that he had not used foreign goods for thirty years. His words are still in my ears, but who would have thought that this farewell would be a final farewell? Alas.

Yarn Market: Sichuan Sales Continue to be Strong, Yarn Market's Rush to Cover Intensifies

The yarn market continues to rise, and the situation is good. Sichuan yarn sales continue to be strong, and the demand for local yarn is very smooth. Yesterday, another 2,200 bales were processed and sent out, boosting morale. Short sellers are rushing to cover, and the market is advancing step by step. However, when the cotton closing price was reached, rumors of negative sentiment arose, and the market fell again. The standard yarn has already closed.

Standard Yarn Rises by More Than Two Yuan

At the opening of the standard yarn market in the morning, the market was stable, with varying differences between months, fluctuating up and down by 2.3 cents. The second round declined, and the third round was even weaker. Unexpectedly, at the closing, it surged by 1.256 yuan. Rumors arose in the market, saying that the issue of circulating notes was being brought up again, boosting morale. However, it was found that large accounts did not have a large amount of goods being dragged in. The general retail investors were panicked. In fact, the Sichuan group's intake of spot yarn continued to be strong. It was found that Senkang, Dafeng, Yutai, and Runkang sold more, while Mingde, Xingchang, Shenji, Wangtai, and Xing bought a lot as well. As a result, this month fell by one cent compared to the previous day, and the long-term rose by 1.11 yuan. The afternoon opening was quite tight, and the buying sentiment in the market was very strong, because the Sichuan group was buying spot yarn, with more than 2,200 bales still being processed. Floating accounts were especially eager to cover, and the price increased step by step. As a result, the near-month price rose by 2.3 cents to 1.8 yuan compared to the morning closing price, and the long-term rose by 0.68 yuan. It was found that Yuda sold 2,150 bales, Tongfu 650 bales, Dafeng 2,900 bales, Senkang 4,400 bales, Runkang 1,400 bales, Mingde 1,100 bales, Shenji 1,100 bales, Taichang 1,550 bales, Changfeng 3,550 bales, and Xiecheng 1,150 bales. Hengyi bought 2,400 bales, Mingde 2,300 bales, Xingchang 2,300 bales, Shenji 2,300 bales, Wangtaixing 1,450 bales, Tonghe 2,150 bales, Juxing 1,250 bales, and Fukang 2,000 bales. Yarn and Cotton Markets Closed on National Day

October 10th is National Day. The standard yarn and cotton markets will be closed for one day according to regulations, and there will be no auctions.

Cotton Buying Sentiment Reinvigorated – Closing Prices Weaker for Forward Contracts –

The cotton market started weak, then became firm, and finally rose again. As a result, forward contracts weakened, but market sentiment was still tight. Due to brisk yarn sales, many parties were dragging in goods and optimistic about the market. Following the yarn market, prices rose step by step, followed by more rumors. At the closing, forward contracts suddenly fell by 25 cents.

Near-Month Cotton Rises Another Half Yuan

At the opening of the standard cotton market in the morning, because U.S. cotton was calm, it rose slightly by two to seven points. Indian cotton fell by 0.25 rupees. Osaka cotton for three products rose by 1.2 cents. The market was ordinary, and the far month fell by 15 cents in the first auction. In the second auction, the near month also fell. Unexpectedly, in the third closing auction, the far month surged by 2.3 cents, saying that the rumors were beneficial, the buying trend was reinvigorated, and the market suddenly tightened. Until the closing, the near month jumped by 4.5 cents. However, the market did not increase batch entry and exit. In fact, Gengfeng exclusively entered 34,000 dan on the previous day, making the table dry. It was found that Changhe continued to sell, and Yuda, Runkang, Xincheng, and Yichang all sold. However, Hexing, Gengfeng, Shenji, Dachang, Mingde, and Fukang all bought. As a result, each month rose by two to five cents compared to the previous day's closing price. At the afternoon opening, because yarn sales were developed, the cotton market rose accordingly. However, by the closing, it suddenly fell back by 25 cents. As a result, the near month rose by 5 cents to 2 cents compared to the morning closing price, and the far month fell by 5 cents. It was found that Yuda sold 9,800 dan, Shenchang 3,300 dan, Taichang 5,100 dan, Runkang 2,900 dan, Xincheng 9,000 dan, Changhe 10,300 dan, Dafeng 1,400 dan, Xinchang 1,900 dan, and Yichang 1,700 dan. Dafu bought 6,600 dan, Jinchang 3,000 dan, Hexing 11,400 dan, Gengfeng 3,400 dan, Shenji 5,300 dan, Dachang 2,200 dan, Fukang 4,050 dan, Fengtai 5,600 dan, and Runkang 4,100 dan. The highest and lowest prices for the day are listed on the left.

U.S. Cotton Demand Can Be Called Active

Yesterday, U.S. cotton opened, with each month falling by 12 points. In the early morning, due to the report being about to be released, the market was stagnant. Cotton farmers were hedging sales, and bulls were closing positions. The weekend weather report was excellent, all of which were the reasons for the market price not rising. Later, colleagues bought, and the market became firm. Industry insiders firmly believe that the movement of new cotton will reach its peak, and the spot demand is active, with a firm and rising base. The cloth market is quiet and beautiful, and factories have already sold until next year, with a limited intention to buy at a price. At the closing, due to short covering, it was still firm and rising, with spot prices rising by three points and futures rising by three to five points. British cotton spot prices fell by seven points, and futures fell by one point. Indian cotton short positions were dumped, and bulls continued to close positions. Cotton farmers sold at Buruch and Pinggul, but colleagues bought on dips. It is estimated that Pinggul and Buruch fell by 0.75 rupees. The price of silver was unchanged. Recorded on the left (5th telegram).

According to a telegram from Bombay, the opening forecast for the 6th was: Bairaoxi at 220 rupees, up 1 rupee; Aomula at 197 rupees, up 1.25 rupees; Pinggul at 156.5 rupees, up 1 rupee.

Piece Goods: Factory Cloth Sales in Southwest China are Relatively Smooth, Selling Prices Rise Frequently and Endlessly

Yesterday, the cotton cloth market remained firm and rising, mainly because the demand from various regions was very smooth, and the selling prices gradually increased. The raw material yarn, thread, and greige fabrics were in short supply, and the urgency of customers' shipments increased. The new cross-transactions were very active. Although the selling prices of various white goods and colored goods were high, they remained the same, and the difficulty of spot goods increased. Yesterday, the Guangdong group fixed orders for more than 200 bales of fine twill, and the newly purchased light and heavy coarse cloth, thread, woolen cloth, straight tribute serge, printed satin, and cretonne were particularly abundant. They were dispatched and loaded at any time, and the current sales in Yunnan, Guizhou, Sichuan, Fujian, and other southwest regions were very active. Spot goods of various cloths were continuously collected, especially the demand for fine twill, fine cloth, thread, woolen cloth, serge, and straight tribute goods from local factories was even stronger. Goods such as blue cloth and Shilin cloth were relatively weak. Secondly, the demand for goods in various ports along the Yangtze River, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other inland regions was also urgent. This was all because of the good harvest this year, the society's economy was slightly relaxed, and the purchasing power was strengthened. In this autumn discount period, it was even more colorful.

Woolen Cloth Prices are High and There are Few Patterns

Yesterday, the woolen cloth transaction was very good, and the standard market price rose sharply. There were not many new patterns arriving, so the goods bought and sold on the market did not have special patterns, and the selling price was too high, so buyers complained that the price was too high, and the goods were incomplete. Rongkang Yuanchang Pinghou woolen cloth sold more than 20 pieces throughout the city yesterday, priced at three yuan. Tianxiang Hanzhong Wang six-foot velvet sold five boxes, priced at 1.6 yuan. Baoke shoe blanket woolen cloth sold more than ten pieces, priced at 7.8 yuan. Dalong Sheep City brand serge sold more than ten pieces, priced at 2.75 yuan. Yuanchang Huanghua special woolen cloth sold more than ten pieces, priced at four yuan net.

Finance: Rumors of Benefits, Standard Gold Price Rises More Than Three Yuan, Large Accounts Seeking Supply is Inconsistent, Market Situation is Very Chaotic All Day Long

Yesterday, the gold market was stable due to the reduction in exchange rates and the increase in raw gold. Large accounts sought supply inconsistently, and the situation was uncertain. Rumors of benefits rose, and the exchange rate fell due to recent weakness. The market situation was fluctuating all day. In the early morning, overseas silver markets in the UK and US were flat, and the forward price of Monterrey silver was unchanged. London raw gold rose by half a penny, and the exchange rates followed suit. The central bank announced that the exchange rates for the UK and US were flat, and the customs gold unit was unchanged. The standard gold price was announced to be 1146.9 yuan, and the off-site preparatory transaction opened and immediately rose to 54 yuan. Hengyu, Taidecheng, and Jiuda sold, while Yuanmao, Yongzhi, Fengyong, Fuxing, and Yongwanxing bought. It gradually rose to around five yuan. The morning opened high, and large accounts came to buy after the opening, and continued to rise. However, short sellers took the opportunity to add codes, and some spot firms sold slightly. HSBC announced that the exchange rates for the UK and US were flat and fell once. The silver equalization tax was announced to be unchanged, and buyers moved together and improved again. However, there was still a lot of struggle in the middle, and short sellers began to turn long, and the trend became firm. However, because large accounts suppressed the price at a high level, the noon situation was peaceful again. Later, the off-site retreated to around 55 yuan. Fuxing, Yongshengyuan, Yongjiu, Dalifeng followed suit and bought, and turned back up. After the opening, because Chinese firms fought to fill in spot US dollars, many parties continued to close out at a lower level and stepped down. However, buyers moved again after the low, and although Indian silver rose by three annas, it was still pulled up. The long party began to unload, and the Indian silver was reported flat twice. As a result, it was hovering. Today, I will record the market situation for the whole day.

Securities: The Situation Changes Unpredictably, Public Bonds Rise Sharply and Return Slightly, Types C, D, and E Rush Out of the 60 Yuan Mark, Transactions are Highly Prosperous Reaching More Than 13 Million

Yesterday, at the Chinese Securities Exchange, the market situation was constantly fluctuating, with rapid rises and falls. Initially, there were rumors that 700 million circulating vouchers would be issued. This statement came from a certain market, but it was ultimately confirmed by the financial community that there was no such thing. The market price fluctuated greatly with the cold and heat of people's minds. Therefore, such baseless rumors also arose with it. The market price rose excessively and fell easily. The future is difficult to be optimistic. Yesterday's opening was very good, with Premier Jiang returning to Beijing, and the negotiation situation should be able to unfold. Numbers 35 and 45, etc., especially retail investors, bought in very eagerly, and there were many who turned from short to long. The market price rose uniformly from 12 cents to 3.5 cents. The second round of trading was good, and number 35 continued to buy without stopping, and number 23 also absorbed a lot, rising again by 12 cents to 4 cents. In the afternoon opening, rumors spread about the issuance of circulating vouchers, and people were fanatical. The strong buying sentiment in the market was the best phenomenon in more than a month. And after many days of rising, C, D, and E all rushed out of the 60 yuan mark, which was especially commendable, and actually rose again by 34 cents to 9.5 cents. At the closing, rumors suddenly arose, and those who were shorting type E were still blindly following, improving by another 1 to 4.5 cents. When the type D was auctioned, the situation suddenly changed, gradually turning from tired to falling. Those who had been long before turned out of the cage, even shorting. Market rumors stated that not only was there no circulating voucher, but there were also other unfavorable rumors. Like the shadow of a snake in a cup, they disturbed each other again, and suddenly fell by 67 cents. Even the most popular type A was unstable and fell by half a yuan. However, the market price result was still a uniform rise, but the difference was too far. Type A was only 35 cents, and type E was actually 1.35 yuan. Therefore, the price change today must still have an amazing phenomenon. The total number of transactions was 13,195,000 yuan. Now I will list the results of its rise and fall in a table for comparison (unit yuan transaction unit hundred yuan)

Grain: Flour Short Accounts Endure Pain to Compete for Coverage, Reversing from Falling to Rising: Far Month Jumps by 4-5 Cents

Yesterday's flour market, after opening in the morning, each month initially showed a falling trend, and in the afternoon it rebounded sharply. With the price of foreign wheat, Chicago fell by 4 cents and Canada fell by 23 cents. Therefore, when quoting prices, the market surface in each month fell by 23 cents compared to the previous day, but the buying and selling transactions were smooth. However, later, although large accounts had allocations, the people's minds were still good, so in the hovering, they returned to one cent higher. Until the afternoon opening, the situation changed greatly again, because the market rumored that the currency system would change again, saying that the circulating vouchers would be announced soon to control the country's economy. Therefore, speculative groups rushed to buy, and short sellers had to endure the pain to compete for coverage, causing the market atmosphere to soar, and compared with the previous day's closing, the far period rose by 35 cents. Looking at the current situation, half is the situation and half is the good sales, so there will be no way to grasp the future.

Wheat Futures Rise After Initial Fall; Distant Months Rise by a Significant Eight Points

Yesterday morning, the Chicago wheat market opened, with prices for all months falling by two, three, or four cents due to wheat quotations from abroad. Moreover, the previous day's increase had been too rapid, making a correction unavoidable. Thus, opening prices for all months were three to four cents lower than the previous day. Later, due to profit-taking by bulls, market sentiment weakened, and prices fell another one or two cents. However, the situation changed dramatically when the market reopened in the afternoon. Initially, the flour market rebounded after falling in the morning. Subsequently, rumors of impending currency reforms led well-known speculative groups to aggressively buy, causing opening prices to jump four or five cents. Later, with strong buying interest, prices continued to rise five or six cents, resulting in a net increase of four or five to eight cents compared to the previous day's closing prices. This situation was entirely influenced by the current political situation. Currently, wheat prices have increased by five to ten cents, as mill demand remains good, and customers are standardizing and selling. Shandong Dali Ji wheat is quoted at 5.40 yuan, Guzhen wheat at 5.39 yuan, Puzhen wheat at 5.17 yuan, Huangqiao wheat at 5.25 yuan, Jiangbei wheat at 5.20 yuan (with a secondary grade at 5.10 yuan), Nanjing wheat at 5.12 yuan (with a secondary grade at 5.02 yuan), Daqiao wheat at 5.22 yuan, Huai'an wheat at 5.30 yuan (with secondary grades at 5.23 and 5.27 yuan), Wuhu wheat at 5.17 or 5.18 yuan, Yao Guan wheat at 5.35 yuan (with a secondary grade at 5.30 yuan), and Weiting wheat at 5.07 yuan. Fuxin purchased 8,000 bags, and Shenda purchased 3,000 bags.

Rice Market in Hexia: Uniformly Higher Prices

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the supply from various sources was again scarce, with a total of just over 4,000 shi arriving at No. 20 warehouse. However, sales were brisk, and broker demand included 1,100 to 1,200 bags of kiln-dried Baige rice from Dalian, Qingdao, and Yantai, along with just over 200 bags of thin and broken rice. Market conditions immediately became active again. The kiln-dried Baige price rose by thirty to forty cents, thick new japonica rice increased by thirty cents, and Du Yang and other varieties of new and premium rice followed, increasing by ten to twenty cents each. Thin and broken rice also recovered by over twenty cents as a result. New Yinyuan rice was in tight supply.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were over thirty sources of supply from Hexia. Various types of rice were in demand on the market. Due to tight market conditions in the city, morning trading was brisk, while afternoon trading was relatively flat. Broken japonica rice increased by ten to twenty cents, and new japonica rice remained tight, rising by twenty to thirty cents. Kiln-dried rice lacked a market. In addition to an increase of ten cents for thin rice, high-quality Yangjian rice increased by thirty cents, medium-quality rice increased by twenty cents, and Dubu premium rice increased by twenty to thirty cents. Bianqian rice remained unchanged, and premium rice was somewhat tight.

Demand and Sales of Customer Xian Rice are Both Strong; Market Prospects Remain Upward

The arrival of customer xian rice totaled over 20,000 bags the day before yesterday, and another 10,000 bags arrived yesterday. However, due to the seriousness of the current situation, sellers were mostly reluctant to sell and pushed prices higher, making the market increasingly firm. The Guangdong merchants have been aggressively buying unpolished rice in recent days. With both arrivals and inventory of unpolished xian rice being scarce recently, the market rose another ten cents yesterday. Other milled rice varieties also showed a slight uptrend. In addition to local merchants and Guangdong merchants, Shantou merchants and North China demand were very keen. Yesterday, Quanzhou merchants also purchased actively, and there was some activity from inland and Ningbo buyers. Therefore, sentiment and market prospects remain continuously upward. Total daily sales included 7,145 bags of Jiangxi rice, 12,000 bags of Zhejiang rice, 4,000 bags of Hubei unpolished rice, and 600 bags of Taiwan early rice.

Drought Makes a Bumper Soybean Harvest Unlikely; Sesame Sales are Slow and Market is Soft

Although it is said that the soybean market enjoys a good annual environment with plentiful harvests, actual reports from production areas indicate that the recent drought has greatly affected the harvest, despite the good quality of the soybeans. As a result, the market supply consists mainly of early-harvested Jiujiang soybeans, which arrive continuously, while other varieties are scarce. Therefore, future prospects are relatively stable. Demand from oil pressing plants remains strong, and sales to South China are also robust. Yesterday, a total of over 6,000 bags of new soybeans from various regions were traded, with prices increasing by five to six cents. Prices for foreign sesame are unchanged. Arrivals of raw goods have increased, but sales are slow, and the market is sluggish. It will be difficult to see improvement in the short term, and we must wait to see how foreign sales develop.

Sugar Market: Sugar Prices Gradually Stabilizing

Yesterday, the sugar market trend turned stable. The guild set the price for No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar for immediate delivery at 21.80 yuan and for transit goods at 6.40 yuan. No. 4 Dongbai sugar for immediate delivery was priced at 21.65 yuan, an increase of five cents, with no other changes. No. 1 refined white sugar from local factories such as Jinxin and Dahua was priced at 20.50 yuan, with Nos. 2, 3, 4, and 5 priced accordingly. Chaozhou merchants offered over one hundred bags of Huanggang Qing at 14.10 to 14.20 yuan, and Dali Zhuang offered one hundred and several tens of bags of Wenmian red sugar at 14.80 yuan, Yihe Zhuang at 14.10 yuan, and Hehe Zhuang at 14.30 yuan.

Dried Goods: Longans Drop Another One or Two Yuan

The arrival of Tong'an longans has gradually decreased in recent days. However, an investigation of the quantity of goods arriving at different warehouses indicates that the total number is still substantial. It was reported yesterday that over one thousand boxes had been sold, falling another one or two yuan compared to previous prices. Larger sizes are sluggish and have not yet been sold.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Firms Still Finding Good Sales for Raw Silk

Yesterday, sales of non-foreign green tea remained sluggish. Morocco's pricing for various types of green tea is very tight, and Russian and American firms are mostly taking a wait-and-see approach. The market remains depressed. Yesterday, only Xiehe Jinlong and other firms purchased a total of over two hundred boxes of Zhenmei and Zhenmei needle tea, with prices remaining flat and weak. Only a few hundred boxes of Qimen black tea remain in stock. The Anhui-Jiangxi Black Tea General Marketing Office is currently busy with settlement matters in order to close down.

According to a report from the Tea Industry Association, the green tea market has come to a standstill after the devaluation of the French franc. There was no significant progress yesterday. However, after several telegram exchanges between foreign firms and overseas buyers, there has been some progress in price negotiations. Yesterday, firms such as Baolong and Xiehe discussed prices for various teas, with Baolong's proposed prices for various Zhenmei teas being closer to acceptable levels. Transactions are expected to occur within the day, and the market may be able to break the deadlock.

Metals: New Japanese Steel Products Arrive in Shanghai in Droves

New Japanese steel products (produced by factories such as Yawata, Osaka, and Nakayama), such as new Yangyuan, angle iron, new Yang plate, T-iron, steel plate, I-beam, and black iron sheet, have recently been arriving at Mitsubishi, Huishan, and other warehouses. It is estimated that the quantity is over twenty thousand dan. However, with limited sales recently, holders of the goods are quite anxious, making it difficult to be optimistic about opening prices.

400 Barrels of Zinc Sheets Sold at Fixed Price

The recent fixed price for zinc sheets is £18 per ton, with 400 barrels sold by a certain British firm. The overseas price will subsequently be £18 4s per ton, so the Shanghai market is exceptionally firm. Furthermore, existing inventory is low, making opening prices even firmer.

Special Article: Reply to Inquiry from Yang Wansheng Grain Shop in Xuzhou

(1) The August export quantity of sesame refers to the quantity that has been inspected for export by the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau.

(2) The table lists the quantity of sesame shipped to the United States as 54.68 quintals, which means 54 quintals and 68 kilograms. Each quintal is 100 kilograms. The "." point used in the numbers in this newspaper's table indicates that the numbers following it are decimals.

(3) The number of quintals that each train car can hold varies depending on the size of the car, ranging from 20 to 40 tons. Each ton is equivalent to 10 quintals. You can calculate it accordingly.

This publication has repeatedly received inquiries from readers, and we are happy to answer them in order to meet your expectations. However, this publication has limited space and cannot publish these replies earlier, which has caused you to wait. We are deeply sorry for the delay. Furthermore, many matters are trivial and inconvenient to disclose in this publication one by one, wasting space. We ask for your understanding. - The Editor

A modern Miss introduced: "This is my 1936 model friend."

The ugliest person is rare because that is the Creator's virgin work.

A descendant of the Qing Dynasty has the alias "Lord of the Red Bean Pavilion." People mishear it and mistakenly think it's a "red-headed devil" with a red cloth wrapped around his head and a face full of scars. The difference in their aesthetic appeal cannot be measured!

What is the purpose of the straw hat on a pedestrian's head on a hot summer night?

Why bother teaching children harmful things? What's suitable for society isn't always...

It's just that asphalt roads in the summer aren't very friendly to the skin. Otherwise, women wouldn't need to wear high heels that expose their heels and toes!

Fighting for a Vote

— Qing Qu

Elections are the best system in all civilized countries in the world. Since the Republic of China, we have held several elections, but they have never been pure. When the Northern Warlords stole power, they turned elections into a pile of dirty history. How shameful! Thinking of the "magic lantern," "bedroll spreading," "coffin overturning," and "corpse swapping" that were rampant in various places at the time, I feel both angry and amused. However, in the end, they simply used money to manipulate everything, which is called "vote buying." From then on, all the good election procedures were swept away.

Now it's different. The election of National Assembly representatives is based on Article 1 of the National Assembly Organization Law, which stipulates that the mission of the Assembly is to "enact a constitution" and "exercise the powers conferred by the constitution." So... how important is the responsibility of the National Assembly representatives? However, the exercise of the right to elect rests primarily on the shoulders of the township and village heads. Therefore, whether the election of National Assembly representatives this time can conform to the public opinion of the people in various regions depends on what kind of people the township and village heads are now electing. Although the election by the township and village heads still needs to be circled by the commissioner and decided by the citizens, it must be known that the choice of election is not easy! Because some candidates invite people for "meals," some even "coerce," and some resort to "surveillance." Therefore, when the township and village heads reach this point, they must use their conscience to deal with it to be worthy of the people.

I remember an incident in Saar, where the decision of returning to Germany or France was to be decided by a referendum. At this time, a German woman living in Shanghai, after hearing the news, immediately took a plane back to fight for a vote. Think about it: she is a woman, and far away from her homeland, not nearby. Because she refused to give up her sacred duty to vote, even though it was just one vote, in terms of numbers, it didn't matter much. But! How could she carelessly ignore it? Therefore, the election of National Assembly representatives must be recognized as a very important page in the history of the Republic of China. Even those who run for election, if they do not use dirty tricks but act with a bright and upright open attitude, will naturally be respected. Who would dare to ridicule and spit on them?

Research on "Bastard"

— Shijiu

Among the words used to curse people, besides all kinds of obscene and unbearable words to insult the other party's mother, wife, sisters, etc., "bastard" is probably the most severe and widespread. The three characters "bastard," when analyzed literally, mean: propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are called the eight virtues; the "loss of eight" means cursing people for losing the "shame" character in the eight virtues, which means "shameless." The word "egg" is like saying "not a thing." Therefore, "bastard" means a shameless thing. This interpretation is probably familiar to everyone and does not need further explanation.

However, using "loss of eight" to interpret "shameless" is plausible, but it seems like reciting scriptures, and it still feels somewhat forced. Why? Most vulgar curses originate from peasants and bumpkins. I ask, what do peasants and bumpkins know about the eight virtues? Recently, I read the fifth chapter of the novel *Unexpected Fate in Zaiyang Hall*, written by Qiu Zhai during the Daoguang period of the Qing Dynasty, which says:

"Kuang Shitang received Yun's letter, opened it and took a look, and was startled. His heart felt like a little deer was bumping inside. He thought to himself, 'This matter must have been caused by the cunning procuress. If there was no such abduction, my matter of buying a concubine would not have been exposed. This time, it won't be difficult to force this procuress to write a bond of reliance, but this matter...' "

In the sixth chapter, Yun demanded a bond of reliance from her husband Kuang Shitang for the cunning procuress, and it was also said, "You should take out the bond of reliance from that procuress." According to this, "bastard" can also be interpreted as "procuress," and it seems that the latter is more colloquial.

"Procuress" means "old procuress." This word is very colloquial. Adding "yellow" is because it's a common surname, just an example. Therefore, "yellow procuress" is like "Wang Po." In short, "yellow procuress egg" means "son of a bitch." Also, when cursing someone as "yellow procuress egg," the words "muddled" are often added before it. "Tent" refers to a bed "tent": "muddled tent" is like meaning that the curtains are not in order, which is similar to "yellow procuress egg," with no distinction between high and low. Therefore, "bastard" is probably a later term, hence this study.

Swapping the Nest of the Luan and Phoenix

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 7: Brotherly Affection Hides Letters, Pities Weak Sister / Heavy Air of Poetry and Books, Peeks at Shadows, Laughs at Poor Scholars

Therefore, Jiang and Zhang corresponded for two or three months, and met no less than a hundred times, but still neither dared to speak first. Fortunately, this secret was not known to a third person, so the two of them could proceed slowly. However, can a secret be kept forever? There is no such thing in the world. In the fourth month after the correspondence, an accident occurred. Guoqi's letters to Menglan were always sent to the school. But by the end of June, it was already summer vacation. If the letter was sent to the school, it would take many days to reach Menglan's hands. He had also guessed from Menglan's reply that she had many female classmates with whom she corresponded. Therefore, he wrote the handwriting on the envelope more beautifully, treating it as a girl's letter, and sent it to Jiang's house. At first, two letters were also delivered to Menglan's hands as usual. One day, Menglan went to a relative's house with her mother and sister-in-law. The men, however, were all at home. At this time, a letter from Guoqi was delivered to Jiang's house. The person who received the letter was an illiterate maid. Without hesitation, she sent it directly to the master's room. Haoran put on his glasses, and was holding a book in both hands, sitting by the window in the sunlight reading. Haoran's eldest son, Wuxuan, was standing beside him, wanting to say something. At a glance, he saw the name of his younger sister on the envelope, and the postscript was signed "Zhang Ji." He suddenly felt a movement in his heart. He remembered that four or five days ago, his younger sister was sitting in the hall, and the old woman outside brought a letter, and he had greeted her in the courtyard to receive it. That shape seemed a little unusual. Looking at the letter again, it was written by Zhang Ji. It seemed that there was no such Miss Zhang among his female classmates. While Wuxuan was thinking like this, he had quickly taken the letter from the maid's hand. Haoran put down the book and asked, "Who sent the letter?" Gexuan replied, "It's a letter from a colleague of mine, asking me to pass it on." Haoran was reading with great interest, so he didn't ask any more questions and continued to read the book. Wuxuan stood in front of his father for a while, then retreated. When he got to his own room, he took the letter in his hand and carefully examined it. Although the handwriting was beautiful, it was definitely not written by a young lady. Moreover, he seemed to have seen this handwriting somewhere before. Although opening other people's letters is not allowed by morality, this matter is quite important. If there is any secret in this letter, the problem would be big if it fell into his father's hands today. So he closed the door, opened the envelope, and read it slowly. After reading it, he quietly pondered for a while, and then tucked the letter into his pocket. When Menglan returned home that day, it was already past 10 PM. Although Wuxuan met her, he didn't say a word. (82)

Qingyang Moon

— Ziwei

I took advantage of the Mid-Autumn Festival's Crown Life Troupe to go to Qingyang Port to enjoy the moon for the third time.

The many lanterns hanging along the iron bridge over the port still emitted colored light. Looking down at the deep blue port water, ruffled by the southeast wind, it formed patterns like fish scales. Several white boats carried young couples, drifting leisurely in the clear stream, relaxed and happy. From afar, the soft singing voice floated from the water, intoxicating, intoxicating a bit of lightness.

Looking up at the azure sky, a round moon, like a bright mirror, hung high, surrounded by a canopy like mist. The floating clouds, pure and clear in the blue sea, were illuminated by the auspicious moonlight, highlighting the layered peaks. At this time, the distant trees became ink spots, and a faint osmanthus fragrance filled the air. This quiet autumn moon, this cool autumn night, brought together many celebrities in one place. What joy, what happiness! I recalled Li Chongguang's line—"The old country is unbearable to look back on in the bright moon"—and couldn't help but sigh.

That night, because I still had some private matters, I took the night train with my wife to my hometown—Suzhou—to join in the scene of reunion. I hadn't been home for several months, and I felt that my stepmother had become much thinner, while my nephews and nieces could already babble and walk by touching the wall. Seeing my late mother's portrait, I wanted to shed tears again. That night was filled with mixed feelings of joy and sorrow, making it difficult to fall asleep.

Tomorrow, I'll visit the owner of Zilan and chat, and also meet my brother Fan Yunshu. I'll accept his invitation for lunch at a restaurant opposite Wuyuan. In the evening, I'll take the car back to Shanghai.

Special Feature

Glimpse of the Yellow Sea

— Feng Kuni

Under a clear sky and a cool breeze, I walked with light steps in the desolate wilderness, on the soft, velvety sand, following the traces of ox carts like iron rails. Then I saw the boundless Yellow Sea.

The wind was fierce, and the clouds in the sky flew quickly towards the other side. The sun emitted golden light. Many fishermen had smiles on their faces, and they were stacking fishing nets onto the carts again. The two oxen that had been lying down resting just now were pulled over again and tied to the carts. They were whipped a few times on their backs, and they roared and pulled the heavy carts forward wearily.

The wind calmed down a little. Standing on the beach, I felt a little unsteady and felt strangely panicked, almost afraid. But the gulls were singing leisurely and playing on the sea. And the eagles were circling over the sea looking for food.

The surging sea tide, from afar, I saw layers of waves rushing towards this side quickly with the wind. Suddenly, there was commotion on the sea, all the waves were pushing, and the prostrate衡 broke the quiet sky. The waves衡 violently hit the sea dike, and the water splashed up several feet high in anger, and the sea water衡 destroyed the soil of the sea dike. The sunlight reflected on the horizon, as if there were many golden snakes dancing on the water.

The huge fishing boats in the Yellow Sea felt small and insignificant, drifting with the undulating sea tide. The masts were raised, and they were returning majestically full of fresh goods. The ox carts on the beach were all going into the sea, gradually submerging the legs of the oxen, gradually submerging the bodies of the oxen, only seeing the noses of the oxen breathing air on the surface of the water.

Suddenly, the waves calmed down, and the waves gradually pushed forward, and the water on the beach receded slowly.

When the tide was receding, the beach was crowded with people, carrying baskets and holding iron hooks. After the tide receded, many crabs, cicadas, clams floated on the beach. They squatted down happily to catch them. They all depended on these many aquatic products to live.

The wind on the beach was a little cool, and my legs were a little sore, so I turned my back to the sun and stepped on the sand that had been soaked in seawater to go back.

Rambling Talk

Shanghai's Miniature Labyrinthine Mansion

— Jiang Gong

The life of Shanghainese people is novel, mysterious, and somewhat comical, not at all ordinary. Just the various situations regarding "housing" are already strange and diverse, showing all kinds of extremes, which is completely unexpected by people from other places. Especially the internal construction of houses, with innovative designs and ingenious ideas, can truly break all records of ancient and modern times, both domestic and foreign. Even architects who have just returned from studying abroad cannot help but be shocked and admire them!

In the past, during the imperial examination era, the lowest form of the eight-legged essay was called the "ink school," which was known for its piling up of redundant words. It specialized in using clichés such as "closing the door and shutting the door, covering the firewood door," "Heaven and earth are the cosmos," and the like, so-called "building houses on houses, stacking beds on beds," which the world spread as a joke. In Shanghai, when you go to many people's homes, you can often see this kind of "ink roll" style of multi-story pavilions, as dense as pigeon cages, smaller than pigeon cages, stacking beds on beds, which is not surprising at all.

It's just because the rent in Shanghai is too expensive, and some people, such as third-hand landlords, want to profit from it. Naturally, they have to think of ideas and come up with tricks in this small house to achieve their goals of supporting their families and making a living once and for all. Some clever second-hand landlords, with their flexible minds and superb skills, can think outside the box and transform an ordinary two-story house into a five-story building, adding more than a dozen bedrooms. Such a large place can accommodate more than a dozen or twenty households. This kind of precise design and superhuman skill can truly be praised as an economic doctor and engineering expert without shame!

The old-fashioned Shanghai two-story residences are usually: inside the Shikumen gate, a small rectangular courtyard, a living room in the front, and a kitchen in the back. There are only two rooms that can be officially used as bedrooms: the living room upstairs and the pavilion room. In Shanghai, honest people have no food to eat! If they honestly rent it out like that, wouldn't the second-hand landlords have to drink the northwest wind? To solve major problems such as food, clothing, marriage, and funerals, in addition to living in the house for free, is impossible unless you dream! But don't worry, they have their own magic!

Their first step is to build a layer of white iron shed above the courtyard, extending the living room straight to the gate, moving the screen wall backward, separating the middle with board walls into two rooms, slightly extracting a narrow aisle on the side, and finally, the space under the stairs can also be separated into a room. Therefore, there are at least three rooms. Needless to say, the kitchen is also being renovated. The living room upstairs can also be divided into two or three rooms according to the method of the lower living room. In the middle of the stairs, a mezzanine made of plywood is usually built. The clever landlords also add a mezzanine in the middle below the living room upstairs and above the living room. Upstairs, it is even more obligatory to add a larger room on the back building. The roof and the sun deck are even more naturally and justly able to add a high floor. This can probably be called a towering pavilion, not within the mezzanine. In this way, at a minimum, three or more floors can be added on top of the original two floors! As for the small mezzanines inside the pavilion room for storing items, there is no need to calculate them in detail. After this major construction, it looks like Emperor Yang of Sui's labyrinthine mansion. Although the sparrow is small, it has all five organs. When the big landlord runs over, he simply won't recognize that this is his house. The second-hand landlord pays the big landlord a rent of only twenty yuan or so per month, while the income is at least seventy or eighty yuan or so. This kind of profit-making method is more wonderful than buying your own property (but that construction fee also costs about a thousand yuan or so, so they are also making a profit on their investment!). It's just that those who are third-hand tenants, with their noses and eyes squeezed together, noisy voices, dirty air, and dirty houses, are too miserable!

The most miserable are those who live in the mezzanines, who don't see the sun all year round. They have to turn on the electric lights even during the day, and they can only sleep sideways and can never stand upright. It's pitiful that they have to bend over and bow their heads and can only be short people for life! In summer, when the wind doesn't blow, the stench is overwhelming, and they often get heatstroke. It's really suffering for paying money. This kind of life is probably not much different from sitting in a death row cell!

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

On Heroes and Success or Failure

— Fang Kewen

Our country's delegation to the 11th World Games has returned. Using the old saying "Don't judge heroes by success or failure," we really shouldn't ridicule and mock the athletes who returned with a score of zero. Moreover, "How our country's sent athletes will perform in the World Games was known long before they went abroad. The reason for participating is to gain experience, and because in the previous Los Angeles World Games, our country only had one participant, this time is the first formal participation. It is deeply hoped that participation will attract the attention of the entire nation... After participating in the World Games this time, the great disparity between the strong and the weak may make the people know what to strive for and what to work hard for." Therefore, we shouldn't ridicule and mock these "defeated" "heroes."

But although the saying "Don't judge heroes by success or failure" can be used to comfort the defeated heroes, it can't be used as a talisman for them. We still have to see how this hero failed and who said this sentence.

How did our heroes fail? "How our country's sent athletes will perform in the World Games?" was "known long before they went abroad." This can't be blamed on the "heroes," but when the news of the World Games came, there were things that exceeded our "prediction," such as in track events, our athletes were eliminated in the preliminary rounds with the last place, and in field events, they didn't even meet the "qualification." In ball games, we were able to win in friendly matches, but we lost to others in official matches. With such a tragic ending, is this what we "predicted" long ago?

It is not shameful for heroes to fail, but failure should also have a justifiable reason. If you usually have the "qualification" to compete with others, and you lose because you are exhausted, then it may be said that although you failed, you are still glorious. But our heroes are usually barely able to get the "qualification," but temporarily don't even meet the "qualification." Can this kind of failure also be "judged" by "Don't judge heroes by success or failure?"

In fictional novels, we often see defeated heroes say to victorious heroes: "After three years, I will come again to learn from you." Heroes who say such things either really go to implement their "gentleman takes revenge in three years" plan from scratch, or use this as a comfort to dispel embarrassment, as a catchphrase to wrap things up. We failed this time, and the "four-year revenge theory" is also being sung loudly. But is this the former or the latter? I dare not think badly, and I don't want to think badly, so let's wait and see after four years!

But in the high-pitched sound of this four-year revenge theory, some people also say, "This failure can also be said to be the main cause of future victory... It is better to be greatly defeated and be able to be self-aware than to be proud of a small victory, and it will not lead to the bad habit of Yelang's self-importance." It is not wrong to encourage the defeated heroes without ridiculing them, but if you give them all kinds of forgiveness, or even say that a small victory is not as good as a great defeat, as if "great defeat" is better than "small victory," I cannot agree with this. Of course, the original intention of saying this is not like this, perhaps it is just the opposite. But if you are proud of a small victory, and you don't reflect on a great defeat, then what? -- We should have the courage to settle our own mistakes.

Saying that you don't reflect on a great defeat may be somewhat arbitrary and close to insulting, but I think it is best to settle this account after four years: to put it another way, let's say you "win small" after four years. If the physical strength of the general public is still like this, relying only on a few "Kings" and "Fish" to hold up the scene, and you don't get a score of zero anymore, that is still a failure, because the way of sports does not exist in creating a few "sports stars," and if the "star system" in the sports world continues to exist, then even if you get a score of zero again, in the country, these athletes with a score of zero will still be unable to avoid "Yelang's self-importance."

Because in the country, they are still the "great generals" in "Shu has no great generals."

Old Locke and Theresa (Continued)

— Lin Na

"Theresa, you can't go on like this, you have to think about your age..." Old Locke looked worried.

"They...they are all so barbaric...Dad...I'm scared!" His daughter's face was red, she mumbled, head down.

"There's no way around it! Think about it, I'm fifty-two this year, how many more fifty-twos do I have left driving a carriage?"

His daughter lowered her head even further, lost in thought, not saying a word, her lips pale and trembling.

One day, Old Locke came home early, sat on a stool and smoked his pipe. His daughter had just returned from the coconut grove, holding a large package of baked bread in her hands, a happy look on her face, a smile on the corners of her mouth, standing timidly in front of him. Old Locke looked at her indifferently, then asked in a surprised tone: "Theresa, what's going on?"

"Guess, Dad..." his daughter said with a smile, looking pleased with herself.

Old Locke couldn't guess, so he shook his head; then she continued, "The baker on the street gave it to us, he said: Theresa, isn't your old man back yet? Didn't he leave you money to buy bread? It doesn't matter, this is my gift to you."

"When did he say that?" Old Locke frowned unhappily.

"He often pulls me into the shop and says that when I pass by! I didn't accept it before, but I did this time..."

"Did he make any advances towards you?"

His daughter's face flushed red, and she mumbled softly: "He...he loves me..." She believed that the old man's face would light up with joy because of this. However, he didn't, he looked very sad, the corners of his mouth trembling, muttering quietly in a desperate tone:

"This is impossible, Theresa..."

He knew the baker, a fat,

Page 18

American man in his thirties. Because of his son's misfortune, the old man always felt a hatred for the white people as rulers. He often said angrily: "They have sucked the blood out of the Filipinos, and now they are imprisoning the old white folks, just so they can have more people doing forced labor for them in prison factories!"

Thinking this, his heart was deeply pained by hatred.

The heavy carriage rumbled over the cobblestone street, and soon stopped outside a bamboo fence. There was light and laughter in the house. The old man frowned, listening quietly on the carriage platform. A sharp male voice caught his attention. He suspected it was coming from that fat baker. So, he stepped over the fence gate and loudly kicked the short wooden ladder leading to the small house. Before long, the baker appeared in the small house, his daughter following behind him with a forced smile. He apologized to the old man, looking flustered and uneasy, and then strode away.

The old man watched him leave with angry eyes, then stood in front of his daughter and asked silently:

"Theresa, what's going on?"

"He came to propose to me, Dad... he knelt in front of me, so pitiful, tears in his eyes, saying, Theresa, marry me, my heart..." The old man impatiently stopped her with his hand:

"What did you say...?"

"I cried too, I agreed... He is a good person...I also...Dad, let us get married."

The old man lowered his head in despair. He thought of his son in prison, and his whole body felt unbearably hot. Finally, as if he had made a great decision, he trembled and said, "You want to marry him, fine, come with me now!"

His daughter climbed onto the carriage with him, and immediately they set off for the beach. That night, the old man drove the carriage back alone, sleeping soundly. From the next day on, no one ever saw Theresa again.

Zhu Zixia's Boat Catching in Costume

Story of the Bamboo Garden

— Shen Jiaqian

It had rained in the morning, but the afternoon was clear. The sky in early autumn was like a smooth leather ball, and the pale yellow sunlight peeked out from the clouds, shining on the lonely courtyard. Mao Sheng drank a little more wine at lunch, grabbed a handful of straw and made straw sandals in the corner of the wall. That was Mao Sheng's special skill. The straw sandals he wore were all made by himself, but the ones he made weren't as durable as the ones he bought, so he was often seen knotting straw in the corner of the wall.

Mao Sheng was an old servant of my family, who had come to my house from my grandfather's time. He must be over sixty now. But when people asked him his age, he just opened his mouth and said, "You guess." When people guessed his age, he nodded, "You guessed right! You guessed right!" He never told people his age properly. When Grandma heard this, she would scold him, "You've lived your age on a dog, you're still as mindless as a child!" He would just laugh and walk away.

Mao Sheng liked to tell stories, so he was especially close to us children. When he made straw sandals, the children always surrounded him.

"Mao Sheng, tell us about the silly son-in-law."

"No, Mao Sheng, tell us about Bao Gong's birth, and how the fox spirit repaid his kindness later?"

"Yes, didn't you say you'd tell it today?"

"Don't吵! Don't吵!" He spread out his hands, asking us to sit down, then raised his eyes and looked at the clouds in the sky, "I'll tell both. First the silly son-in-law, then the fox spirit repaying his kindness."

So he began to tell stories, starting with "Once upon a time there was a silly son-in-law..." one after another, until it was time to cook dinner and he hadn't finished half a straw sandal.

Today, the children had run off to play at someone else's house. Mao Sheng seemed to feel a little lonely. He was half-heartedly making straw sandals, his eyes often raised to the sky, as if "Once upon a time there was a silly son-in-law..." was about to fall from his mouth.

I crept up behind him and covered his eyes with my palms, asking him who it was.

"It's the young master, I know it without looking. Why don't you go out and play?"

"They've all run off, where can I go to play?" I sat down next to him.

"Good!" He swept away the straw, as if he hadn't intended to make straw sandals in the first place, "I'll take you to play, to dig for bamboo shoots in the bamboo garden."

"Don't talk nonsense, there aren't any bamboo shoots now." I didn't believe it. If you don't... follow me to dig; he grabbed my hand and led the way, taking two... from the corner of the wall, giving one... to me...(To be continued)

Movies

###

In the future, more films suitable for Chinese tastes will be shown. The Cathay Theatre on Avenue Joffre, with its magnificent architecture and complete equipment, has already been praised by word of mouth, and it is said to be unique. The reservation... other first-run theaters are the same. However, this theater seems to focus on Westerners. Now, because the number of Western residents is increasing day by day, and the number of Chinese audiences in this theater is also increasing day by day, in order to facilitate Chinese movie fans in the future, the theater has decided to change its policy and show more films suitable for Chinese tastes. For example, "A Filial Son Murders His Father" I Give My Life, which is being shown today, is an example of their new plan. The story of this film is adapted from a famous stage play that caused a sensation in the United States for two years. It is sad and touching enough to earn people's tears, and its tension makes the audience breathless. The leading actors are Sir Godfrey Tearle, Francis Drake, and Tom Brown, three major stars, who perform a tragic and moving performance, which is indeed a work worth appreciating.

Li Minghui and "Qingming Season"

Li Minghui, this long-absent artist, has joined the Star Film Company and her first film is starring in Ouyang Yuqian's "Qingming Season". This is a work that exposes the evils of inheritance and focuses on the entanglement of women in feudal families. Li Minghui plays a maid who is oppressed in an old family; she initially loses her pure chastity due to the seduction of the owner of the family, and then suffers beatings from the mistress and abandonment from the owner. At this time, she already has a child. This poor child, as soon as he is born, encounters a fierce and cruel face, and the vicious methods of the villains. From this, a moving story develops.

Since starring in "Woman", Li Minghui, who has been silent on the screen for a long time, is playing an oppressed woman here; changing her past style, and collaborating with the great director Ouyang Yuqian, she is achieving extraordinary achievements.

Grand Cathay Presents "Song and Dance on the Road to Success"

Is a Great and Luxurious Song and Dance Film

The Grand Cathay Theatre originally scheduled to open "The Blood Case at the Racecourse" today (Wednesday), but due to special reasons, it temporarily changed to showing "Song and Dance on the Road to Success" Sirg Baby Sing, produced by 20th Century Fox. The story of the film alludes to the interesting history of film star John Barrymore pursuing a young girl. In addition to Alice Faye and Adolphe Menjou, there are also a large number of comic singers and movie stars who have joined, which are novel and unique, and are also rare on the screen. This film is no different from a grand gathering of stars, a base camp of song and dance, and a general mobilization of laughter. It can be called second to none in song and dance films.
